## D54 — RUN-K Q&A CHARTER EXPANSION: 31 locked decisions, reprioritizing toward the TACTICAL ENGINE — [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-14)
A 10-round / 31-question popup session (Aaron) pre-cleared the forward path. **HEADLINE: the real-time UG:G tactical engine is now PRIORITIZED ahead of S3–S5.** The locked answers (carry into every future run; also in memory `civilwar-q-a-charter-runk`):
- **Direction:** tactical engine SOONER (ahead of S3–S5); alt-history = **fully player-driven** (the sim follows, NO historical thumb on the scale — supersedes the old "consensus-favored" framing); the "your war vs history" tracker = a lightweight **readout + divergence-log FIRST** (zero-regression).
- **Tactical engine:** **BOTH** gridless-real-time **AND** hex-turn as **selectable modes** (Classic stays frozen, never regressed); first slice = **First Bull Run, one full battle** (deploy→maneuver→fire→morale→result); combat = **UG:G-style** (morale + flanking/rear + cover + fatigue, **low micro**, few unit types); controls = **drag-to-maneuver, low-APM**; unit scale = **regiments / brigades** (the existing OOB data feeds it); **FULL strategic conditioning via the bridge + a tactical-only FREE mode**.
- **Graphics — BATTLE LAYER FIRST:** linked-assets = **embed links + mandatory offline (procedural) fallback**; PD sources = **Library of Congress + Internet Archive + Wikimedia Commons**; concentrate the animation budget on the tactical engine.
- **Survival/loot:** apply to **ALL modes** (campaign march legs + tactical battlefield loot + a dedicated march/survival mode + free-battle/skirmish); survival depth = **light, preset-gated** (off by default, dial-able, §27); loot = **STANDALONE rarity-tiered loot** (Borderlands-style drops with its own inventory) — NOT only Armory-integrated.
- **Architecture/efficiency:** **SINGLE HTML + linked assets** (confirmed — it's the best for sharing: email the one file OR host one URL; multi-file/bundler would break the $0/double-click deliverable); **group `src/` into subsystem folders** (src/strategy/, src/tactical/, src/render/, …; keep NN load-order within each); **perf presets + profile hotpaths** (Auto/Low/High, instancing/LOD/culling) for the Intel UHD 617 floor.
- **Sharing/saves/onboarding:** hosting **deferred** (keep it buildable + ready to send; GitHub Pages later on request); saves = **localStorage + named slots + export/import** (portable saves); onboarding = **accessible default + skippable tutorial**.
- **Depth/breadth:** theaters = **Eastern + Western** (defer naval/riverine/trans-Mississippi — buildable later, not a priority); battles = **add the canonical big ones, THEN a custom-battle builder**; deepen **Politics/Congress/home-front + Logistics/supply/railroads** most.
- **Quality engineering:** add a **full-campaign playthrough probe** to the no-regression suite; **adversarial bug-hunt every milestone, scaled to size**; **build a reusable historical-data layer** + an **in-game sources codex** + keep the **web-grounded multi-agent Verified/Inferred** research pattern.
- **Education/a11y/audio/done:** WCAG 2.2 AA = **one big dedicated S4 pass** (build fast now, comprehensive audit later — Aaron does a11y professionally); audio = **period music + battle SFX + UI cues, all accessible** (toggles/captions/volume, never gates play); **it is a PERPETUAL personal project — NO fixed v1.0** (ship vetted milestones forever; "done" is whenever Aaron's happy).

## D55 — RUN-K Q&A SETS 2–3: 39 implementation-level decisions (the deep-everything build spec) — [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-14)
Two more popup sets (Set 2: 30 Q; Final: 9 Q) cleared the implementation forks. **THROUGH-LINE: MAXIMALIST depth on every system (Paradox-grade deep sim across all axes) — but preset-gated / delegable so the simple UG:G core still stands alone (§27). Aaron favors a TOGGLE for every play-style option.** (Also in memory `civilwar-q-a-charter-runk`.)
- **Tactical engine (the next work):** runs on the **existing 3D terrain engine** (PBR/HDRI/post-FX), not a fresh 2D map. Fog = a **toggle, default OFF** (light-LOS / full as options). Enemy AI = **scripted-historical + reactive**. Formations = **line/column/skirmish + facing, drag-set**; morale/rout = **CENTRAL** (waver/break/rout/rally; flanking shatters cohesion). Casualties = **realistic-grim, tasteful, toggle-able**; tone = tasteful-educational default with an **unflinching/graphic toggle**. Time = **active auto-pause, toggle** (pause+speed / active-pause / real-time). Command = **direct + delegate brigades to AI**. Victory = **objectives + morale collapse + time**. Units = **low-poly 3D models** high-tier, billboards/counters as the perf-preset fallback. **P0 NEXT SESSION = a SANDBOX skirmish first:** ~2 brigades/side, one terrain, the full core loop (deploy→drag-maneuver→fire→morale/rout/rally→win), then scale to First Bull Run. Pacing: battles ~15–30 min; campaigns span sessions.
- **Loot/survival:** loot = **many tiers + randomized affixes** (Borderlands-deep), affects **weapons + supply + morale items**, and is a **MAJOR supply source** (capture/foraging strategically central; the cash-poor CS leans on it) — still §27 preset-gated. Survival activities = **mini-games** (hunt/fish/forage/scavenge); pressures = **rations + weather + disease, light** default (full-attrition as a dial-up); dedicated mode = an **Oregon-Trail-style journey between battles**.
- **Graphics/audio:** art = **period-realistic** (PD photos + painterly 3D + engraving UI); footage = **contextual cutaways at key beats** (skippable, offline→procedural fallback); animation budget = **battle layer first**; audio = **period music + battle SFX + UI cues, all accessible**.
- **Strategic depth (all DEEP):** **Politics** = Congress + war legislation + factions/parties + governors/states + elections-beyond-1864; **co-equal politician/commander, fully delegable**. **Home front** = a **deep social sim** (population, classes, the collapse of slavery, refugees/contrabands, the wartime economy). **Logistics** = **full operational logistics** (railheads/depots/wagons/rivers + interdiction) + a **dedicated rail-management layer** + an **in-battle supply mechanic**. **Economy** = a **deep economic sim** (sectors, labor incl. enslaved-labor collapse, prices, trade). **Diplomacy** = a **deep diplomacy sim** (Britain/France recognition, King Cotton, Trent). **Cavalry/recon** = a real system: **screen, scout, raid** (Stuart/Forrest/Sheridan; ties fog + logistics + named-generals).
- **Knowledge/teaching:** **one queryable historical-data knowledge base** (single source of truth, provenance-tagged) feeding **ambient cards + a browsable codex + a seminar mode**; alt-history tracker = **divergence log + consequences + a graded final report**.
- **Structure/meta:** **single HTML + linked assets** (best for sharing); **group src/ into subsystem folders**; **perf presets + profile hotpaths**; saves = **localStorage + named slots + export/import**; presets = **play-style presets + per-system sliders**; **SP-first now**, but **design for mod-friendly data + shareable saves/scenarios + eventual hotseat/async MP**.
- **Scope/finish:** theaters **Eastern + Western** (naval/riverine/trans-Miss deferred); **canonical battles, then a custom-battle builder**; **historical + what-if scenarios**; **both short + grand campaigns**; a **playable Reconstruction phase** + a graded epilogue; **PERPETUAL project — no v1.0**.

## D56 — RUN-K TACTICAL ENGINE P0: the real-time SANDBOX skirmish (the D54/D55 reprioritization — tactical FIRST, ahead of S3–S5) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The very next milestone after S2 per D54/D55: the first real-time, gridless, UG:G-style tactical layer, built as a **sandbox skirmish first** to PROVE THE LOOP before scaling to the First Bull Run slice. Shipped `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` (the new `tactical/` subsystem folder, manifest path `tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`) + `tools/probe-field.mjs`. The full core loop runs: **deploy → drag-maneuver + facing → line/column → fire → morale/rout/rally → charge → win/lose**, on a procedural 3D field, with low-APM controls, reactive-lite enemy AI, active-pause + 1×/2×/4×.

**Architecture (decided + logged):**
- **D56.0 SIBLING engine, not a mutation of the hex-bound `__M3D`.** The shipped "Modern" 3D renderer in `build/base.html` (§23, ~line 10460) is hardwired to the hex board (`G.battle.M`, `colrowToPixel`, hex tiles) — it is literally a 3D re-skin of Classic, exactly as `MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md` §3 warned. So `__FIELD` owns its OWN THREE scene + camera + RAF loop + full-screen DOM root (`#fldRoot`), completely OFF the Classic / `__M3D` code path → **zero regression risk** (probe-verified: the sandbox never writes `G.battle`/`G.campaign`/`G.mode`). It reuses the SAME three@0.128 stack (via the base `_m3dLoadScripts` loader) + the sunlit-field art direction; deeper PBR/HDRI/post-FX reuse is deferred to P1+. This honors D55's "runs on the existing 3D terrain engine, not a fresh 2D map" in spirit (same 3D tech stack) while keeping P0 isolated.
- **D56.1 Renderer-agnostic sim + a MANDATORY offline 2D fallback** (D54): the sim state is pure data; a 3D renderer draws it when THREE loads, a 2D top-down canvas renderer draws it when THREE is unavailable (offline). All combat formulas are PORTED from the base engine (`moraleCheck`/`resolveFire`/`resolveCharge`, base ~1015-1086; ratings `_OVR_WEIGHTS` ~10126) — not reinvented — then adapted to continuous, positional, per-tick resolution. A seeded LCG RNG makes probes reproducible + balance tunable.
- **D56.2 Additive launch via a MutationObserver** on `#sheetPad` (NO override of `openMainMenu`). **Bug found by the bug-hunt:** the first cut anchored on `.menu-grid`/`#mmFree` — but those exist only in the SHADOWED `openMainMenu` (base ~3249); the LIVE menu is a later broadsheet redeclaration (~8346) using `#gnFree`/`.gn-col`, so the button never injected and the whole module was UI-unreachable. Fixed to anchor on `#gnFree` and inject a native `.gn-btn` into the Field-Dispatches column; `probe-field` now has a MENU-ENTRY regression step (the gap that let it through — the probe drives `fldLaunchSandbox()` directly).
- **D56.3 Subsystem folder grouping STARTED, full reorg deferred.** This module proves the D54 `src/` subfolder grouping (`tactical/`); reorganizing the existing 22 strategy modules into `src/strategy/`, `src/render/`, etc. is its own dedicated milestone (don't conflate a big path refactor with a big feature — revertibility + regression surface).

**Adversarial bug-hunt** (6 dimensions × diverse-lens [correctness + real-world-impact] skeptic verify, **60 agents**, ~3.3M tokens) → **24 confirmed of 27, all fixed** (3 correctly refuted). Deduped to ~16 unique:
- **HIGH:** (1) the dead menu anchor above; (2) exit/relaunch during the async THREE load resurrected a torn-down sandbox (leaked GL context / null-canvas `getContext` crash) → a **launch-generation token** (`__FIELD._gen`) makes stale loader callbacks no-op, bumped in `fldExit`; (3) end screen keyboard-inoperable + Tab hijack → `fldKey` yields on `phase==="over"` and only steals Tab mid-battle, focus moves to the rematch button, `role="dialog"`; (4) 2D fallback silently blank when 3D init throws after the WebGL context bound → `fldResetCanvasForFallback` swaps in a fresh canvas (a canvas that took a GL context can't switch to 2D).
- **MED:** deploy + AI-fallback facing constants pointed sideways (every front mis-scored as a 1.5× flank) → corrected to the `atan2(dx,-dz)` convention (0=north, π=south), so brigades face the enemy; mutual-charge resolved melee twice per tick → unordered-pair guard; column frontage 0.7 reduced casualties even on flank/rear (inverted enfilade) → arc-dependent (0.7 head-on, 1.4 enfiladed); 3D unit facing rendered 180° backward (`-facing+π` → `-facing`); per-frame `THREE.Color` alloc → hoisted cached colors; double-launch RAF guard in `fldStartLoop`; `fld2dInit` defensive on a null canvas; color-only side ID → a non-color cue (2D "U"/"C" letters; 3D cube vs pyramid finial — full CVD/pattern pass is the dedicated S4 a11y milestone, D54); space/enter on a focused button double-fired → `fldKey` ignores button targets.
- **LOW:** `fld3dDispose` now disposes OrbitControls + `forceContextLoss` (context exhaustion over repeated rematch); `fldExit` now removes the window-level `pointerup`/`resize` listeners; `_fldAiClock` reset in `fldInitSim` (cross-launch determinism); dead `ammoF` made a real low-ammo fire taper; `fld2dView` scale clamped (no negative draw scale on a tiny viewport); a 1-frame resize flicker fixed (`fldResizeCanvas` repaints the 2D canvas after the clear).

**Balance auto-tune (charter §8.7, logged):** `FLD.FIRE_BASE` 7.4 → **3.2** (peak cas/s, full-strength rifle brigade, close) — the primary fight-length knob. With the facing fix removing the universal mis-scored 1.5× flank multiplier, the 2-brigade-a-side loop settles at ~**90s** at 1× (maneuver ~30s → firefight → rout cascade), a morale-driven break (the losing side breaks at ~10-15% casualties — the UG:G feel) rather than a bloodbath. Battle length is set by the morale-break cadence, not the fire rate (2.7 and 3.2 both give ~90s); 3.2 keeps casualties from going bloodless. Full battles (the P1 Bull Run slice, more brigades/bigger map) will run longer.

**Tooling:** `tools/probe-field.mjs` — **13/13**, 0 pageerrors, GPU-flake-free (asserts the renderer-agnostic sim headlessly: deploy→4 units, maneuver, fire-both-sides, ≥1 rout, a declared winner [no deadlock], no NaN, determinism, victory-by-collapse, objective-hold accrual, clean re-launch, the 2D fallback DOM/draw/teardown, the live-menu button injection, no Classic contamination) + a confirmed mid-battle 2D screenshot. **Also bumped `tools/t1probe.mjs` goto timeout 30s → 60s** (the suite standard) — pre-existing tightness exposed by the 1.45MB file's `load`-event wait on the THREE CDN + offline 404s; not a game regression (Classic paints; all 60s-budget probes green). Full no-regression: **24 probe suites green, 0 pageerrors, diag-classic Classic paints.** Deliverable ≈**1448KB**.

## D57 — RUN-K TACTICAL ENGINE P1a: the FIRST BULL RUN scenario (real OOB + historical terrain + the rail-pivot reinforcement timeline) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The next slice after D56's P0 sandbox: the FIRST real historical battle on the `__FIELD` real-time engine — **First Bull Run (First Manassas), July 21, 1861**, brigade scale, on a historical-terrain field, with the **rail-pivot REINFORCEMENT TIMELINE as the teaching mechanic**. Selectable from the field menu ("⚔ BATTLE — FIRST BULL RUN (1861)") next to the sandbox button. New `data/bullrun.json` (the engaged main-field OOB distilled from `HISTORICAL-DATA.md`, provenance-tagged, anti-Lost-Cause) + new `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (the scenario module) + minimal seams in `T0-field-sandbox.js` + new `tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` (15 steps + a 3D-leak guard). Deliverable ≈**1485KB**.

**Architecture (the design judge-panel verdict — 3 approaches scored, A "guarded T0 seams" won 8.9 vs B 6.7 / C 7.8):**
- **D57.0 EXTENSION via guarded T0 seams, NOT an override of the sim loop.** T0 exposes no-op-by-default seams keyed on `__FIELD.scenario`/`reinforce`/`attacker` (all null/"sandbox" by default): `fldInitSim` dispatches to `fldScenarioInit` (early-return); `fldSimStep` calls `fldScenarioTick` (per-tick reinforcement splice); `fldInjectMenuButton` → `fldInjectScenarioButtons`; `fldOnOver` → `fldScenarioEndHtml`; terrain readers/renderers generalized to multi-hill/multi-wall + markers via `fldHills()`/`fldWalls()` accessors (single-hill sandbox value-identical); `fldCheckVictory` made reinforcement-aware + asymmetric. **The sandbox path stays byte-behavior-identical → probe-field held 13/13 throughout** (+ a terrain GOLDEN-SNAPSHOT guard grafted from approach C catches silent sandbox-geometry drift). T1 **orchestrates only** (terrain build + OOB instantiation + arrival splice); it never duplicates combat/morale math — every per-unit computation flows through T0's unchanged leaf helpers (grafted from approach B), so a future T0 balance fix reaches Bull Run automatically.
- **D57.1 The rail-pivot REINFORCEMENT TIMELINE.** The battle is modeled as ARRIVAL WAVES (the historical engagement): at T=0 only the lead Union brigades (Burnside, Porter) contact the Confederate delaying force (Evans, Bee, Bartow) on Matthews Hill; both sides then FEED brigades over the morning — the Union across Sudley Ford, the Confederates rallying on Henry House Hill and receiving rail-borne reinforcements (Jackson @135s "Stonewall", Stuart @180s, Early @220s, Elzey @275s "off the train" onto Chinn Ridge, the Union right). 9 brigades/side total (2+3 at T=0, 13 in waves). Reinforcements spawn IN ARRAY ORDER at scheduled sim-times with ZERO spawn-time RNG (determinism). A side is "destroyed" only with no live units AND no reinforcements still detraining (`fldArmyPending`).
- **D57.2 ASYMMETRIC victory (attacker seizes, defender denies).** The Union (attacker) wins by seizing-and-holding Henry House Hill (`holdToWin`) or breaking the CS army; the Confederacy (defender) wins by denying the hill to the time limit or breaking the US army. `__FIELD.attacker`/`defender` from data; null for the sandbox (symmetric, unchanged). `__FIELD.winBy` records destroy/hold/timeout.
- **D57.3 Historical terrain + atmosphere.** Henry House Hill (the objective crest), Matthews Hill, Chinn Ridge (3 hills), the Robinson House lane (wall cover), 5 woods, + labeled markers: Bull Run creek, Young's Branch, the Warrenton Turnpike, Sudley Springs Ford, the Stone Bridge, "to Manassas Junction" — rendered in both 2D and 3D. A pre-battle BRIEFING modal (situation + objective + 2 teaching cards + provenance), arrival BANNERS (color-coded, stacked, role=status + aria-live), and an end-screen "Your war vs. history" teaching payoff (divergence note + 3 cards with provenance).
- **D57.4 Subsystem-folder grouping continues** (`src/tactical/T1-*`); the full strategy-module reorg stays deferred (D56.3). **Deferred to P1b/P1c:** the hex-mode toggle, full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario, deeper PBR/HDRI/post-FX, and a CS player side.

**Balance auto-tune (charter §8.7, logged):** `holdToWinSec` **75 → 140** and `timeLimitSec` **600 → 480** in `data/bullrun.json`. 75 let the CS auto-hold the rear objective (it sat on Henry Hill) and win at ~76s before the timeline engaged; 140 makes the full rail-pivot timeline engage in the typical battle (all 13 reinforcements arrive; sweep at hold140 = battles 262–472s, every seed). The asymmetry probe proves the rail pivot is LOAD-BEARING (removing ONLY the CS reinforcements drops the Confederate outcome score sharply: the Union is denied to ~262s WITH the trains vs ~239s/easier WITHOUT, csScore 252611 vs 223884). timeLimit 480 trims the dead-attrition tail after the last reinforcement (275s) so the denial-win turns more on the timeline. **KNOWN/LOGGED for P1b:** AI-vs-AI auto-battle currently leans Union (the attacker AI grinds effectively; the CS defender AI doesn't reliably counterattack) — the primary mode is human-Union-attacker racing the timeline; CS-favorable balance (smarter defensive/counterattack AI, the fog-of-war toggle aiding the defender, force re-tuning) is a P1b item.

**Adversarial bug-hunt (loop-until-dry):** Round 1 = 6 dimensions × diverse-lens default-refute verify + completeness critic (**27 agents, ~1.6M tokens**) → **14 confirmed of 20, ALL FIXED**: HIGH — missing-`data.objective` crash (guard hardened to fall back to sandbox), the briefing-Esc-tears-down-the-battle bug (overlay keydown stops Esc propagation + traps Tab), focus yanked off the briefing button by the deferred `fldRoot.focus()` (guarded against an open modal), `fld3dBuildUnits` leaking GPU geometries/materials on every reinforcement rebuild (dispose-before-detach; probe-confirmed bounded: 21 geoms after all 13 waves vs 51 at wave 1). MED/LOW — stale `__FIELD.scenData` leaking the Bull Run title into a later sandbox (nulled in the per-launch reset), the rally-aware gone-check (scenario-only; sandbox byte-identical) + comment overstatement, and `__FIELD.winBy` recording + 4 probe false-confidence gaps closed. Round 2 = the completeness critic surfaced a REAL gameplay bug the probe missed (it only ran `autoBoth:true`): in the real game (player=Union) **US reinforcements spawned `ai:false` with a default hold order and idled in the rear** → now a player-side arrival auto-marches toward the objective on spawn (the player can redirect). Also fixed: clustered same-tick arrivals clobbering the aria-live region (batched into one announcement) + a Bull Run objective coordinate drift-guard. Every fix re-probed green.

**WCAG 2.2 AA (charter §8.18; wcag-auditor on the new UI):** 8 non-text-contrast border fixes (warm-umber borders lightened to ≥3:1 on both surfaces, aesthetic preserved), a `:focus-visible` outline injected for the tactical buttons (11.25:1), `aria-modal="true"` added to the end dialog, and a Tab focus-trap added to the end screen. Body-text contrast already cleared 4.5:1.

**Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK → **probe-bullrun 15/15 + 3D-leak guard, 0 pageerrors** (asserts: full engaged OOB, the 3 named hills + Henry House Hill objective + markers, reinforcements on-schedule/in-order/idempotent, player reinforcements advance, the full battle reaches the reinforcement era with a recorded winBy, the defender-denial timeout win, the rail-pivot load-bearing asymmetry, determinism, the sandbox golden-snapshot unregressed, no Classic contamination, the 2D path, scenario a11y, the live-menu button, 3D geometry bounded) → **full no-regression suite GREEN (25 probe suites + t1probe 14/14 + bootprobe + diag-classic Classic-paints, all 0 pageerrors)** → probe-field **13/13** (P0 sandbox unregressed). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: TACTICAL P1b** — the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS defensive/counterattack AI + the fog-of-war toggle · full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario · deeper 3D (PBR/HDRI/post-FX). Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3 alt-history, S4 education/codex/WCAG-AA pass, S5 victory + Reconstruction.

## D58 — RUN-K TACTICAL ENGINE P1b-i: the FOG-OF-WAR toggle (the UG:G recon pillar) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The first slice of the P1b bundle: fog of war on the `__FIELD` real-time engine — a per-side line-of-sight visibility model, **a toggle, default OFF** (D55; MODERN-UGG-PLAN §5). Sub-divided from P1b as the single highest-value deep slice: a marquee UG:G system that ALSO directly engages the logged AI-leans-Union balance gap (fog aids the defender). All in `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` (shared by the sandbox + Bull Run) + `tools/probe-fog.mjs`. Deliverable ≈**1495KB**.

**Architecture (decided + logged):**
- **D58.0 A GATED visibility model, default-OFF = a byte-identical no-op.** `__FIELD.fog` (a persisted toggle, `G.settings.tacticalFog`). `fldVisible(side, target)` returns `true` immediately when fog is OFF, so every gate below is a no-op and the sim/render/AI is byte-behavior-identical to the pre-fog engine (probe-field held **13/13**, probe-bullrun **15/15**, diag-classic green). Fog ON: `fldComputeVisibility()` runs once per tick (and is primed at launch for the deploy screen) building `__FIELD.vis = {US:{}, CS:{}}`; `fldAcquireTarget` + `fldAiUnit` skip non-visible enemies (you can't fire at / react to what you can't see); the 2D + 3D renderers hide unscouted enemies from the US player; the HUD shows only *sighted* enemy brigades. Determinism: visibility is position-based, **no RNG**.
- **D58.1 Sight by arm + woods block line-of-sight.** `fldUnitSight` — cavalry scout widest (720 yd) > artillery (470) > infantry (430): cavalry-as-recon, the seed for the later cavalry system. `fldLosClear` uses an **exact segment-vs-woods penetration model** (sum the sight-line length inside each woods disk; blocked past `WOODS_SEE_THRU` = 75 yd) — robust where a fixed-sample walk failed both ways (a thin grazing chord stays visible; a line straight through is blocked; two units in the same woods still see each other up close).
- **D58.2 Last-known "ghosts."** A faded dashed marker + "?" at an enemy's last-seen position once it goes out of sight (`__FIELD.lastSeen`), purged on the unit's death so a destroyed brigade leaves no phantom. 2D for this slice (3D ghosts deferred).
- **D58.3 The toggle.** A "Fog: On/Off" control-bar button (with `aria-pressed`) + the **V** key + the persisted setting; an aria-live announcement on flip.

**Teaching + balance (charter §8.7, logged):** fog ON **flips the Bull Run AI-vs-AI outcome to a Confederate denial win** (probe-confirmed: winner CS by timeout) — the Union advances blind into the unseen reverse-slope (Jackson) and the rail reserves (Early/Elzey) and can't seize-and-hold in time. This is the historically-correct result AND it directly addresses the D57-logged "AI-leans-Union with fog OFF" item: fog is the defender's friend. No numbers changed (fog is purely the new visibility layer); default OFF keeps the prior balance.

**Adversarial bug-hunt (loop-until-dry):** 5 dimensions × default-refute verify + completeness critic (**17 agents, ~0.9M tokens**) → **11 confirmed (deduped to 5 root causes), ALL FIXED**: HIGH — a destroyed enemy left a permanent phantom "?" ghost (purge `lastSeen` in `fldKill` + harden the `fld2dGhosts` skip-guard to `!live || !live.alive || visible`); MED — fog-ON-at-launch blacked out the whole DEPLOY screen because `__FIELD.vis` wasn't computed until the first sim tick (prime it at the end of `fldResetRun`, the shared launch chokepoint); MED — `fldLosClear`'s 7-sample walk leaked LOS through grazing woods chords AND over-blocked two units inside the same woods (→ the exact penetration model above); MED — the fog toggle button lacked `aria-pressed`; LOW — the no-selection "N Rebel brigades sighted" HUD line was frozen (throttled refresh from `fldRenderTop`). probe-fog grew 11→**13/13** with a dead-enemy-ghost step + a deploy-visibility step.

**Verification:** GATE OK → **probe-fog 13/13, 0 pageerrors** (default-OFF no-op · LOS math · hide-far/reveal-near · woods-block · cavalry-scout-widest · AI/targeting-only-visible · ghosts purged on death · deploy-visibility primed · toggle persists · fog-ON sandbox+Bull Run resolve deterministically · no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN (26 probe suites + t1probe + diag-classic Classic-paints, 0 pageerrors)** → probe-field **13/13** + probe-bullrun **15/15** (the fog-OFF invariant holds) + a fog screenshot inspected (hidden CS reserves, the sighted-count HUD, the Fog:On button). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: TACTICAL P1b continues** — the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS defensive/counterattack AI (now fog gives the defender the edge; the counterattack AI is the complement) · full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario · deeper 3D (PBR/HDRI/post-FX). Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## D59 — RUN-K TACTICAL ENGINE P1b-ii: the ACTIVE AUTO-PAUSE toggle (the UG:G low-APM pillar) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The next P1b slice: active auto-pause on the `__FIELD` engine — the battle pauses at decision points (a brigade breaks / is destroyed / reinforcements arrive) so a low-APM player keeps up. **A toggle, default ON** (the accessible low-APM default, §8.15; D55 "active auto-pause, a toggle"). A "Auto-pause: On/Off" control-bar button + the **P** key + the persisted `G.settings.tacticalAutoPause`; the pause reason shows in the phase indicator + an aria-live announcement. All in `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` + `tools/probe-autopause.mjs`. Deliverable ≈**1500KB**.

**Fork (decide-&-log):** chosen as this firing's slice over the heavier remaining P1b items (hex-mode toggle, CS counterattack AI, bridge conditioning, deeper 3D) for the best value-to-risk-to-context ratio — a named UG:G pillar that is self-contained, deterministic, and architecturally low-risk; the heavier items stay queued.

**Architecture (D59.0):** auto-pause lives **ONLY in the RAF loop** — `fldStartLoop`'s step snapshots `{routEverCount, aliveCount, units.length}` before the fixed-timestep accumulator and calls `fldAutoPauseScan(...)` after it. The headless probe stepper (`fldStepN`) and every probe `runToEnd` call `fldSimStep` directly and **never reach the scan**, so headless probes + determinism are untouched **by construction** (auto-pause sets `__FIELD.paused`, which `fldStepN` ignores — it gates on `phase`, not `paused`). Default ON via `G.settings.tacticalAutoPause` (unless `===false`); the toggle persists it. `_apReason` lifecycle: reset in `fldResetRun`/`fldInitSim`, cleared on resume.

**Adversarial bug-hunt (loop-until-dry):** 4 dimensions × default-refute verify + completeness critic (**10 agents, ~0.5M tokens**) → **4 confirmed (3 distinct), ALL FIXED**: MED — turning auto-pause OFF while it actively held the battle paused did NOT release the pause (the escape control didn't escape) → `fldToggleAutoPause` now releases an active auto-pause on OFF; MED (a11y) — the durable pause reason wasn't recoverable by AT (only a transient announce) → the Resume button's `aria-label` now carries the reason; LOW — a same-frame death + reinforcement masked the "destroyed" reason in the net headcount (still paused reliably — `units.length` is monotonic-up — but mislabeled) → robust per-frame kill detection (`killed = prevAlive − (aliveNow − spawned)`) + a combined multi-reason announcement. probe-autopause grew 11→**13/13** with a same-frame-mask step + a toggle-OFF-release step.

**Verification:** GATE OK → **probe-autopause 13/13, 0 pageerrors** (default ON · scan pauses on break/destroy/reinforce · same-frame death un-masked · no-op when nothing changed · early-return when already paused · resume clears the reason · toggle OFF releases an active pause · toggle flips+persists · **headless battle UNAFFECTED + determinism** · 2D button aria-pressed · no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN (27 probe suites + t1probe + diag-classic Classic-paints, 0 pageerrors)** → probe-field **13/13** + probe-bullrun **15/15** + probe-fog **13/13** (all unregressed). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: TACTICAL P1b (continued)** — the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · smarter CS defensive/counterattack AI · full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario · deeper 3D (PBR/HDRI/post-FX). Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3–S5.

## D60 — RUN-K TACTICAL ENGINE P1b-iii: the ROLE-AWARE AI — a smarter CONFEDERATE DEFENDER doctrine (closes the logged "AI leans Union" gap) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The next P1b slice and the named complement to fog (D58): a real DEFENDER doctrine for the `__FIELD` real-time engine. The shipped AI was **symmetric** — both sides ran one "advance toward the objective" heuristic (`fldAiUnit`), so the Confederate *defender* played like an attacker: it drifted off its good ground, deep-fled when shaken, and never disciplined a counterattack. That is exactly why AI-vs-AI leaned Union (logged in D57/D57.4/D58). This milestone makes the AI **role-aware**: in an asymmetric scenario the defender HOLDS the objective's forward face in cover, conducts a fighting withdrawal, and counterattacks disordered attackers on a leash. All in `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` + `tools/probe-ai.mjs`. Deliverable ≈**1509KB**.

**Architecture (decided + logged):**
- **D60.0 ROLE-AWARE DISPATCH, gated on `__FIELD.attacker` — the symmetric SANDBOX is byte-behavior-identical by construction.** `fldAiUnit` now dispatches: in an asymmetric scenario (`__FIELD.attacker` set) the DEFENDER side (`u.side === fldEnemy(attacker)`) runs the NEW `fldAiDefender`; the ATTACKER side and BOTH sandbox sides run `fldAiGeneric` — the **verbatim old `fldAiUnit` body**. The sandbox has `attacker === null`, so `fldAiDefender` is **unreachable** there → zero behavior change (probe-field held **13/13** + the terrain golden snapshot). Unlike auto-pause (D59, which had to live in the RAF loop), the defender doctrine lives in the **headless sim path** (`fldAiUnit` ← `fldSimStep` ← `fldStepN`), so it is **fully probe-testable** — including a deterministic AI-vs-AI balance sweep. Determinism preserved: no RNG in the AI.
- **D60.1 A STABLE defensive frame (not the momentary threat bearing).** The defender's spatial frame is anchored to the battle geometry — forward axis = the crest toward the **attacker's home edge** (`fldHomeEdgeZ(attacker)`; the engine models the two armies on the ±z home edges, so the approach axis is z and lateral frontage is world-x), `face` still tracks the nearest visible enemy (aim, don't move). The first cut derived the frame from the *rotating nearest-enemy bearing*; the bug-hunt proved that collapsed the whole line onto one point on a **flank threat** (Chinn Ridge — which this scenario is built around) and **flipped the advance/hold gate** when an attacker crossed the crest (stranding rear reserves). The stable frame fixes both by construction.
- **D60.2 Five branches, hold points clamped INSIDE the objective.** (1) SURVIVAL — wavering + a stronger enemy close → a fighting withdrawal to the reverse slope, still facing the threat. (2) COUNTERATTACK — steady + a **catchable (wavering-only)** disordered enemy within `CTR_REACH` that has closed on the hill + a **dual leash** (the target AND the defender's own position both bounded near the objective) + local parity (`CTR_RATIO`) → charge. (3) DELAY — a unit forward of the line holds and fights to buy time, falling back only when locally outnumbered (`DEF_FALLBACK_RATIO`). (4) ADVANCE — a rear reinforcement marches up to the line (column if far). (5) HOLD — on the forward face in cover, face the threat, pour fire. Every hold/move-to-line point is **clamped inside `obj.r`** so a holding defender actually DENIES the objective (not parks ~237yd outside the 140yd ring).
- **D60.3 Constants (charter §8.7 — logged):** `AI_LOCAL_R=360` (local force-balance radius), `DEF_FACE_FRAC=0.55` (hold-line forward of the crest), `DEF_LANE=1.6` (lateral spread, ×OBJ_R, pre-clamp), `DEF_HOLD_TOL=50` (the on-the-line band), `DEF_FALLBACK_RATIO=0.6` (delaying-force withdrawal trigger), `CTR_REACH=175`, `CTR_LEASH=150`, `CTR_RATIO=0.9` (counterattack gates). A test-only hook `__FIELD._aiGenericAll` (default false, reset per launch in `fldInitSim`) forces generic-for-both so `probe-ai` can A/B the doctrine on identical seeds.

**Balance auto-tune (charter §8.7, the A/B sweep, 8 seeds, logged):** with the **old generic-for-both AI** the CS lost **0/8** fog-OFF (a Union sweep — the logged gap, now empirically confirmed) and **1/8** fog-ON. With the **defender doctrine** the CS wins **8/8** fog-OFF and **8/8** fog-ON. The mechanism is the historical one: **denial/timeout wins** — the determinism check (seed 909) ends at the 480s limit with the Union *still holding more men* (US 17900 vs CS 11731) but unable to seize-and-hold Henry House Hill in time, exactly as McDowell's army failed in 1861. **Decision (decide-&-log):** keep the corrected geometry; a CS-dominant AI-vs-AI is **historically faithful** (First Bull Run was a decisive Confederate victory) and is the intended hard challenge for the **human-Union primary mode** (the player out-micros the AI and has concentration/timing/targeting the generic attacker AI lacks). The prior pre-clamp 5/8 was an artifact of bug #5 (defenders holding *outside* the objective they were denying); the now-correct defender honestly dominates the weak generic ATTACKER AI. **The complementary lever is a smarter ATTACKER AI (concentration / flanking) — logged as the next AI item — NOT weakening the now-correct defender.** Also logged: a smart defender and fog are **SUBSTITUTABLE, not strictly additive** defender levers (fog also blinds the defender's own reactivity) — the D58 "fog flips Bull Run to CS" claim was relative to the *old* AI; with the smart defender the CS already wins fog-OFF, so fog adds little (corrected the stale `probe-ai` header claim).

**Adversarial bug-hunt (6 diverse lenses × default-refute verify + a completeness critic, 27 agents, ~2.3M tokens):** → **10 confirmed (9 finder + 1 critic), ALL FIXED** (10 refuted). ENGINE: **#1/#2 (MED, geometry)** the rotating-bearing frame collapsed the line on a flank threat + flipped the advance/hold gate → the **stable frame** (D60.1); **#5 (MED, behavior)** hold points landed up to ~237yd outside the 140yd objective → **clamp inside `obj.r`** (D60.2); **#3 (MED, edge)** the defender chased **routing** targets it can never catch (rout 62yd/s > charge 30yd/s) and walked off the hill → **catchable (wavering) targets only**; **#6 (LOW, critic)** the leash bounded only the *target's* distance, so a retreating wavering attacker walked the defender off the hill → a **dual leash** also bounding the defender's own position; **#4 (LOW, regression)** `_aiGenericAll` wasn't reset on launch → reset in `fldInitSim`. PROBE-FIDELITY (false-confidence, `probe-ai.mjs`): the COUNTERATTACK step's leash sub-test was actually decided by `CTR_REACH` not the leash, and `CTR_RATIO` was untested → rebuilt with isolated reach/target-leash/own-leash/catchable/ratio sub-tests (#6/#7/#3); the FIGHTING-WITHDRAWAL step couldn't distinguish withdrawal from the delay fall-through → added a `tz < crest` discriminator (#8); the ADVANCE step never exercised the bearing-flip → added a visible-attacker-on-crest guard (#2); the header overstated "fog compounds" → corrected to "substitutable" (#9). (One verify agent erred on `API Error: Overloaded` for the "bearing-flip strand" finding — independently confirmed by #1/#2 and fixed by the stable frame, so nothing was lost.)

**Verification (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK → **probe-ai 11/11, 0 pageerrors** (routing/dispatch · all 5 defender behaviors incl. the bearing-flip guard + the dual-leash/catchable/ratio counterattack gates · the A/B balance sweep fog OFF+ON · the lever matrix · determinism · the sandbox no-op · no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN** (probe-field **13/13**, probe-bullrun **15/15**, probe-fog **13/13**, probe-autopause **13/13**, + the strategy suite + bootprobe + t1probe + diag-classic Classic-paints, **0 pageerrors**). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: TACTICAL P1b (continued)** — the **smarter ATTACKER AI** (concentration/flanking — the complement that restores AI-vs-AI variety, logged above) · the hex-mode toggle (Classic frozen) · full owner-mode bridge conditioning into the scenario + a tactical-only FREE mode · deeper 3D (PBR/HDRI/post-FX). Then P2–P5, loot/survival, S3 alt-history, S4 education/codex/WCAG-AA pass, S5 victory + Reconstruction.

## D62 — PHASE A · CONNECT THE TWO LAYERS: the strategic-desk army now FIELDS in the real-time tactical battle, which feeds back into the campaign — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The first V1-CHECKLIST item (D61 Phase A). The owner-mode war and the real-time tactical engine were two disconnected layers; this milestone is the connective tissue. New `src/tactical/T2-campaign-link.js` (the whole Phase A module) + tiny guarded seams in `T0-field-sandbox.js` / `T1-bull-run.js` + a bridge-briefing button in `src/85`. Deliverable ≈**1545KB**.
- **A1 — conditioning the tactical brigades from `bridgeArmy(C)`.** `fldCampaignCondition`/`fldCampaignConditionUnit` scale the PLAYER side's men + morale + fatigue and RE-ARM a fraction of the infantry from the bought loadout (`C.armory.loadout` → engine WEAPONS key via the `59-armory-field` `_afEngineKey` mapping + the engine era gate). **Anchored at the fresh-campaign baseline 74, band ±12% (`strengthMul` 0.88–1.12), identical to `_a6Condition` (D47.1) and the auto-resolve edge (D48)** — so all THREE battle modes (real-time, Classic-hex, auto-resolve) condition equivalently and a no-investment army plays ≈ the nominal scenario. Reinforcements are conditioned too (T1 `fldReinforceSpawn` seam). Runs from the shared `fldResetRun` hook; no-op when `campaignCtx` is null.
- **A2 — launch from the bridge + a FREE skirmish.** A new **"Fight in real time ⚔"** button on the pre-battle briefing (beside Auto-resolve + the Classic "To the Field") → `fldLaunchCampaignBattle(C)`. First Bull Run (US player) routes to the historical `bullrun1` scenario; every other campaign battle gets a CONDITIONED procedural brigade fight derived from `bd` (us/cs/atk/year/feat; brigade count `clamp(2+round((total−15000)/15000),2,5)`, men `clamp(round(total/(count·5)),1300,2100)`, holdToWin 36s). Plus a **custom FREE SKIRMISH menu** (`fldSkirmishMenu`) — pick side / army size / ground / year / fog — injected as a main-menu button.
- **A3 — result feedback loop.** `fldCampaignComputeOutcome` derives the REAL casualty fractions (men lost / men fielded per side via `maxMen`, correctly counting arrived reinforcements + destroyed units) from the FINISHED fight; `fldCampaignApplyOutcome` builds a CONDITIONED hex roster via `startBattleRuntime`, applies those fractions with `_arApplyCasualties`, then drives the engine's own `campaignAdvance` → `_t1Resolve` (manpower/clock/strategy/enemyWill/victory). **So a real-time win/loss is SUBSTITUTABLE for a Classic / auto-resolved result** (MODERN-UGG §2) — win advances the chain, loss enters recovery, casualties feed the strategic tick. Mirrors the proven `bridgeAutoResolve` (87) pattern; deterministic (no RNG in conditioning or outcome — the fight is seeded in T0). Aborting (Esc) before the battle ends returns to the briefing, re-launchable, nothing advances.
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) the tactical OOB is a faithful ABSTRACTION (a handful of brigades a side; absolute men are abstracted, the loss FRACTION is what feeds back) — a 1:1 regiment port is unnecessary for the layer-connection and is deferred. (b) the campaign First Bull Run routes to `bullrun1` only for a US player (the scenario is built US-attacker); a CS player / a recovery-defend re-fight uses the procedural battle (the CS-player tactical mode is Phase B / fork #10). (c) the same 74-anchor across all three battle modes is deliberate — zero double-count, balanced equivalently.
- **Standalone byte-identity (zero regression by construction):** every T0/T1 seam is a no-op when `campaignCtx` is null and `opts.skirmish` is absent → the sandbox / menu Bull Run / fog / auto-pause / role-aware-AI paths are behavior-identical (probe-field **13/13**, probe-bullrun **15/15**, probe-fog **13/13**, probe-autopause **13/13**, probe-ai **11/11** all held). Classic never touched (diag-classic paints, nonBlank 346).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (6 diverse lenses × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, 26 agents):** → **7 confirmed (deduped from 12 raw; 17/18 verdicts confirmed), ALL FIXED:** **F1 (HIGH)** Esc on the campaign end-screen discarded the decided result (aborted via `_returnFn` instead of resolving — save-scummable; war never advanced) → `fldKey` Escape now RESOLVES on a finished campaign battle (mirrors the button), only mid-battle Esc aborts; **F2 (HIGH a11y)** the campaign end dialog was `aria-modal` with no focus trap (the campaign branch returned before the standalone trap) → added a Tab trap on the single `#fldCampReturn` button; **F3 (MED a11y)** the skirmish menu dropped focus to `<body>` on every option click → restore focus to the chosen chip after the re-render; **F4 (MED a11y)** the option chips used `role=radio`/`radiogroup` without arrow-key roving → switched to a `role=group` button group with `aria-pressed` (matches the click/Enter/Space model); **F5 (MED)** the re-arm `armPlan` was sized to the initial line only, so the running `_armIdx` exhausted before reinforcements detrained (player reinforcements unarmed by the loadout) → `infN` now counts scheduled player-infantry reinforcements too; **F6 (HIGH)** `C.flipAtk` was consumed at LAUNCH but the path is abort-relaunchable → an Esc + re-attempt (any mode) lost the recovery role-flip → flip is now computed for the fight but consumed only at RESOLUTION (`fldCampaignApplyOutcome`), preserved on abort; **F7 (MED)** the Bull Run route ignored a flipped `bd.atk` (a recovery-defend re-fight launched as a US attack) → `_fldCampaignScenarioFor` returns null on `C.flipAtk` (procedural honors the flip). Re-probed green.
- **WCAG 2.2 AA (wcag-auditor on the new UI):** the new surfaces were already compliant (the consistent #745e3f/#766040/#715e3e border palette + the #e8c84a focus ring carried over) — only 2 trivial `type="button"` additions; text ≥11:1, non-text borders ≥3:1, focus rings ≥3.6:1, keyboard-operable, ARIA correct, non-color selection cue (bold + outline).
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK → **probe-campaign-link 16/16, 0 pageerrors** (A1 strong>fresh>weak men + the 74 anchor; loadout re-arm player-only; standalone not conditioned; A2 Bull-Run-route/procedural/skirmish builder/the briefing button; A3 real fractions + win-advances/loss-recovers + the strategic tick + determinism; F5 plan-spans-reinforcements; F6/F7 flip preserved-on-abort + procedural-route + consumed-on-resolve; no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN** (tactical 5 suites + the 22-probe strategy suite + bootprobe + t1probe + diag-classic Classic-paints, **0 pageerrors** throughout). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: Phase B — TACTICAL DEPTH** (B1 the smarter defender-favored ATTACKER AI with the fog inversion tuned out [fork #2] · B2 officers/command · B3 in-battle logistics · B4 distinct arm roles · B5 difficulty presets · B6 the CS-player "command either side" mode [fork #10]).

## D64 — PHASE B-1 · the smarter DEFENDER-FAVORED ATTACKER AI (fog AIDS the defender) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The first Phase B item (V1-CHECKLIST B1; charter fork #2). The complement to the P1b-iii defender doctrine: a real ATTACKER doctrine `fldAiAttacker` in `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`, dispatched to the scenario ATTACKER side (the symmetric sandbox + the defender are byte-identical — fldAiAttacker is unreachable when `__FIELD.attacker===null`). Productionizes the run-k prototype (`ATTACKER-AI-PROPOSAL.md`) with Aaron's locked answers. Deliverable ≈**1552KB**.
- **The doctrine:** a covered defender wins a long-range fire trade, so the attacker CONCENTRATES on the objective's weaker (thinner) flank, CLOSES, and ASSAULTS with the bayonet (melee + numbers beat fire + cover). 4 branches: SURVIVAL (wavering + a stronger enemy close → fall back to rally) · ASSAULT (charge a visible disordered defender always; press the bayonet on a steady defender once CLOSED with local superiority — fog OFF only) · SUPPRESS/PROBE (in fire range without the odds → hold + fire in line while the mass forms) · CLOSE (advance on the weak flank, assault-column when committed fog-OFF, line otherwise). Deterministic — no RNG.
- **Lock (a) — GRADUAL commitment (fixes the prototype's knife-edge):** the assault is a PER-UNIT, LOCAL-concentration decision (`localSup`: `friendMen >= foeMen * effLocal` over the VISIBLE foes, where `effLocal = ATK_LOCAL_RATIO·clamp(1/globRatio, 0.75, 1.4)` smoothly modulated by the global force ratio + an `ATK_GLOBAL_FLOOR` sanity gate). The army commits incrementally as it masses on the flank — NOT the prototype's all-or-nothing global ratio flip (`ATK_ASSAULT_RATIO` 1.5→1.7 phase-transition).
- **Lock (b) — FOG AIDS THE DEFENDER (charter fork #2; consistent with D58):** UNDER FOG the attacker NEVER mass-assaults a position and never column-rushes (it can't trust its sight — a hidden reverse-slope reserve / rail-borne brigade may hold the hill); it advances cautiously in LINE, trades fire / probes, and only exploits a VISIBLE BROKEN unit. So fog denies it the unseen-close melee win and lets the concealed reserves maul the piecemeal advance — it never BENEFITS from fog. The prototype INVERTED here (a concealed column closed unseen and won); tuned OUT.
- **Constants (charter §8.7 — logged):** ATK_CHARGE_R 170 · ATK_ASSAULT_R 130 · ATK_ASSAULT_STANDOFF 70 · ATK_LOCAL_RATIO 1.1 · ATK_GLOBAL_FLOOR 0.85 · ATK_FLANK_BIAS 0.5. Test hooks `_aiGenericAll` / `_aiGenericAtk` (reset per launch) A/B the doctrines in isolation.
- **Balance A/B sweep (8 seeds, Bull Run AI-vs-AI, CS=defender win count — logged):** both-generic (pre-doctrine) fog-OFF **CS 2/8** (US sweep — the gap) · defender-only (D60) **8/8** · **both doctrines (B1) fog-OFF 6/8, fog-ON 8/8**. So Bull Run stays **CS-FAVORED** (historical) but **competitive** (the US breaks through 2/8 fog-OFF) — a bloody real fight (defender casualties **4592** vs the passive attacker's **1276**, ~3.6×), and **FOG AIDS THE DEFENDER** (6→8, the inversion gone). Decision (decide-&-log): the human-Union mode is the primary one (the human IS the attacker there + out-plays the AI); AI-vs-AI is the diagnostic, and a CS-favored AI-vs-AI is historically faithful.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (4 diverse lenses × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, Opus per D63):** → **2 findings, BOTH FIXED:** **#1 (HIGH — broke lock (b))** a single visible picket flipped the `seenOnObj`-based `blind` flag false, letting the attacker assault into the hidden mass behind it → REFACTORED: dropped the picket-foolable `blind`/`seenOnObj` and gated the mass-assault + column-rush DIRECTLY on `!__FIELD.fog` (under fog the attacker is unconditionally cautious — strictly more conservative, no sight-based hole). **#2 (LOW)** the now-removed `ATK_FOG_PROBE_R` had a doc/code radius mismatch → deleted with the refactor. Re-sweep post-fix: fog-OFF unchanged (CS 6/8, byte-identical), fog-ON CS 8/8 (attacker now even more cautious under fog — def-cas 1848, fog robustly aids the defender).
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK → **probe-ai 15/15, 0 pageerrors** (routing · the 4 defender behaviors [unchanged] · the attacker ASSAULTS-when-sighted-closed-local-sup · the attacker CAUTIOUS-WHEN-BLIND · the B1 balance lock [fog-OFF CS-favored, fog-ON ≥ fog-OFF, bloodier-than-passive] · determinism · sandbox no-op · no Classic contamination) → tactical no-regression GREEN (probe-field 13/13, bullrun 15/15, fog 13/13, autopause 13/13, diag-classic paints nonBlank 346, 0 pageerrors). The change is confined to T0's AI (the new fn + the dispatch + constants + the probe) — no strategy module touched, so the 22-probe strategy suite (green in D62 minutes earlier) cannot regress. Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: Phase B continues — B2 officers/command · B3 in-battle logistics · B4 distinct arm roles · B5 difficulty presets · B6 the CS-player "command either side" mode (fork #10, makes this attacker AI player-facing).**

## D65 — PHASE B-2 · OFFICERS & COMMAND on the tactical field (leaders with command radius + can be hit; ties named-generals) — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The 2nd V1-CHECKLIST Phase-B item (D61). Leadership now lives ON the real-time field. New module `src/tactical/T3-officers.js` (the whole layer) + guarded T0 seams (`__FIELD.officers` gate; build at `fldResetRun`; a step before morale; a `(u.cmdBonus||0)` read in `fldMoraleStep`; 2D/3D render + HUD + end-screen hooks; a `commander` field on units) + the Bull Run command cast in `data/bullrun.json.leaders`. Decide-&-log per D61 (cleared scope, no contradicting fork → no pause). Deliverable ≈**1585KB**.
- **The system:** named field leaders ride with their army; each projects a COMMAND RADIUS — friendly brigades inside it recover morale faster, hold longer against the rout (capped save), and rally from a rout sooner (the historical rallying role). Leaders CAN BE HIT: riding near the firing line accrues EXPOSURE; past a hidden, seeded fate threshold a leader is WOUNDED (aura halves) then FALLS — the aura dies and nearby troops take a one-time command shock (the general-down rout trigger: Bee/Bartow, A. S. Johnston, Reynolds).
- **Gated + BYTE-IDENTICAL:** fully behind `__FIELD.officers` (default ON every live launch). The field/bullrun/fog/autopause/ai/campaign-link probes set the sticky `__FIELD._officersOff` → no leaders built, `fldOfficersStep` never runs, the `(u.cmdBonus||0)` reads are exactly 0 → all 6 baselines stay BYTE-IDENTICAL (the new layer is provably the only change). The officers' own coverage = `tools/probe-officers.mjs`.
- **Ties the named-generals layer (S2 m5):** a campaign player commander's field quality + name come from `bridgeArmy(C).leadership` / `cmdActiveGeneral(C)` — the general you appointed rides the field. Scenarios carry the real cast: McDowell/Heintzelman (US) vs Beauregard/Johnston/Bee/Bartow/Jackson (CS).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (52 agents — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 1 confirmed (3/3) + 7 critic gaps, ALL FIXED:**
  - **(HIGH) over-lethal death model** — empirically the army commanders who SURVIVED First Bull Run died nearly every game (anti-citation-grade), the "cost of command" reduced to noise. ROOT CAUSES: a monotonic risk RATCHET (no decay) + no cover term + too-high base rate. FIX: per-leader HISTORICAL `fate` (Bee/Bartow fall-prone, army cdrs durable) + risk DECAY out of contact + wound RECOVERY + a COVER term (`fldCoverAt` — rescues the Jackson reverse-slope lesson) + steep f² falloff + a per-tick exposure cap + lower `HAZ_RATE`. Result: army commanders survive **10/10** seeds; a fall is a rare, history-weighted hinge.
  - **(HIGH) Bee's "stone wall" line fired BEFORE Jackson arrived** (Bee fell 37–96s; Jackson lands 135s) — an anachronism AND a Lost-Cause framing leak (asserting the contested canonical quote as settled fact). FIX: `teachReq`/`teachAlt` gate the Jackson clause on him being on-field, and the wording is softened to the contested framing (matching the `br_stonewall` card).
  - **(HIGH) player-side hardcoded to US** — the HUD roster + fog visibility assumed US; a CS-player campaign would show the ENEMY roster and leak its command status under fog. FIX: `fldPlayerSide()` (CS in a CS campaign, US standalone) drives the roster + fog — prep for B6.
  - **(MED) balance swing + weak probe** — the layer materially shifts the winner; the probe's `>=` assertions were too weak. FIX: moderated the aura (§27) + lowered `CMD_BONUS_CAP` 1.2→0.9 so a dense cluster can't saturate the line into near-immunity; the probe now asserts CS-favored + fog-aids-defender + officers-HELP-the-command-advantage-side + low ON/OFF flips, with determinism locked separately.
  - **(MED) cover ignored / (MED) a11y false narration / (LOW) degenerate aura assertion / (LOW) no fog memory for fallen leaders** — all fixed (cover term; survivors rarely fall + softened to an incapacitation register, only Bee/Bartow keep a fatal register; far-apart falloff test points; `_everSeen` keeps a once-seen FALLEN enemy commander marked under fog).
- **Balance (officers ON, 8-seed Bull Run AI-vs-AI, CS=defender wins):** bare **5/8** → officers-ON **7/8** fog-OFF (CS-favored — the historical command stand on Henry House Hill — but the US attacker keeps a 1/8 breakthrough, preserving the B1 path) · **8/8 fog-ON** (fog still aids the defender — no D64 regression). Deterministic; PRINCIPLED (officers help the side with the denser command), not a re-roll.
- **Verified (full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK → **probe-officers 15/15, 0 pageerrors** → full no-regression GREEN (field 13/13 · bullrun 15/15 · fog 13/13 · autopause 13/13 · ai 15/15 · campaign-link 16/16 — all byte-identical; diag-classic paints nonBlank **346**; bootprobe + t1probe ok; 0 pageerrors) → wcag-auditor clean (1 border-contrast fix) → render visually confirmed (the false-death banner cascade gone; generals survive). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: B3 in-battle logistics (ammo + fatigue depth + supply) · B4 distinct arm roles · B5 difficulty/realism presets · B6 the CS-player "command either side" mode.**

## D66 — PHASE B-3 · IN-BATTLE LOGISTICS (the ammunition economy: supply trains + resupply + exhaustion) + the FOG-CULMINATION fix — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The 3rd V1-CHECKLIST Phase-B item (D61). The real-time field gains an AMMUNITION ECONOMY + deeper fatigue. New module `src/tactical/T4-logistics.js` (the whole layer) + guarded T0 seams (`__FIELD.logistics` gate; build at `fldResetRun`; a step in `fldSimStep` before the AI/fire; an override seam atop `fldAiUnit`; a `(u.exhausted)` move-penalty read in `fldStepMovement`; HUD/end-screen/2D/3D hooks) + the Bull Run `supply` block in `data/bullrun.json` + `tools/probe-logistics.mjs`. Deliverable ≈**1608KB**.
- **The system:** each side fields a rear **ammunition train** with a finite battle **reserve**. A DISENGAGED brigade (no enemy within `RESUPPLY_COMBAT_R`=240) within the train's reach refills its cartridge boxes, draining the reserve; when the reserve runs dry the army "runs low" (the 20th Maine's bayonet charge — out of cartridges). A brigade OUT (≤CRIT=8) falls back to its train UNLESS it holds the objective (then it fires dry → bayonet). **Exhaustion:** fatigue>84 → SPENT → a deeper move penalty.
- **The balance design:** the **ATTACKER's train sits FAR behind its start line** (`fldSupplyRearPos` r+400 — it outruns its supply, Clausewitz's culminating point) and the **DEFENDER's just behind the objective** (r+120). Ties the strategic SUPPLY: the battle reserve scales with `bridgeArmy(C).supply`; a raid-supply order cuts the enemy's. **Gated + BYTE-IDENTICAL** behind `__FIELD.logistics` (the 7 baselines + officers set the sticky `_logisticsOff` → no trains, the step/AI-override/exhaustion never run → byte-identical). Determinism: no RNG.
- **THE HIGH FINDING — the FOG INVERSION (surfaced to Aaron per D61-R1; charter fork #2 — fog must aid the defender):** the bug-hunt empirically found that with **FOG ON**, logistics INVERTED the D58/D64 "fog aids the defender" teaching: Bull Run AI-vs-AI fog-ON went **CS 8/8 → 0/8**. Mechanism (isolated by forcing reserves to 0 → 8/8 restored): under fog the fight is a long fire-trade, and the ATTACKER cycled fresh brigades to its **safe far-rear train** to sustain fire — and a long fire-trade favours numbers (attacker) over cover (defender). **Surfaced** (a HIGH finding contradicting a shipped teaching). **Aaron weighed two fixes:** his first pick (a "defender's-depot" resupply) **provably did nothing** — toggling it on/off gave IDENTICAL results, because the defender was never the ammo-bottlenecked side (its reserve sat ~230 untouched). The ONLY lever that works is **choking the ATTACKER's resupply under fog** (`FLDL.ATK_FOG_RESUPPLY` = 0 — "an attacker advancing blind cannot run its trains forward; it fights with what it carries"). A **SHARP threshold** (even 0.15 leaves the inversion; only ~0 restores it). **Aaron approved the attacker-fog-choke.** Also KEPT the **fog-gated scan** (the resupply/pullback enemy-scans now skip enemies the side can't SEE — consistent with D58/D64, no acting on hidden info). **Result: logistics is balance-NEUTRAL in BOTH fog states — fog-OFF CS 5/8, fog-ON CS 8/8, each matching its no-logistics baseline.** A new `probe-logistics` FOG REGRESSION GUARD step locks it (CS ≥6 fog-ON; currently 8/8).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (64 agents, ~3.3M tokens — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 9 confirmed of 14 candidates + 2 confirmed critic gaps (of 5), ALL ADDRESSED.** 1 HIGH (the fog inversion, above) + LOW probe-fidelity/correctness: the probe comment `RESUPPLY_COMBAT_R (110)`→(240) rebuilt as a **boundary test** (blocked at 230, refills at 250); the BALANCE assertion made **two-sided** [4,6] (was a one-sided floor, blind to over-favouring — the layer's headline risk); `fldSupplyRearPos`'s attacker-far/defender-near asymmetry was **untested + bypassed by Bull Run's hand-authored data** (it IS live in campaign skirmishes) → a new probe step; `fldSupplySeen`'s fog enemy-train reveal **untested** (every step ran fog-OFF) → a new fog-ON reveal step; STRATEGIC TIE asserted only ordering → now pins the **supply curve** + the no-campaign nominal (and reconciled the T4 comment: `sup` = bridgeArmy value, not raw warroom); [critic] a **reinforcement-only side built no train** → `fldSideHasUnits` now scans the reinforcement schedule + a probe guard. Two REFUTED findings were re-evaluated against the code: the routing-enemy guard PERTURBED the 5/8 baseline (→4) so it was NOT applied; the fog-visibility guard WAS applied (correct + part of the fog fix).
- **WCAG 2.2 AA (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** 1 fix — `fldLogisticsHudReserve` `#cf7a5a`→`#d28466` (the `opacity:.8` blend dropped it to 4.23:1 → 4.60:1); all other HUD colors ≥4.5:1, the end-screen border ≥3:1; the 2D/3D wagon sprite colors left (decorative map markers).
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1608KB) → **probe-logistics 14/14, 0 pageerrors** (build/off-builds-none; resupply + reserve drain; close-action boundary pinned at 240; finite reserve; the AI resupply doctrine; exhaustion; the strategic supply-curve + raid + nominal; the fog-OFF balance band CS 5/8; **the FOG REGRESSION GUARD CS 8/8**; procedural asymmetry; fog reveal; reinforcement-only-side train; sandbox no-op; no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN** (probe-field 13/13 · bullrun 15/15 · fog 13/13 · autopause 13/13 · ai 15/15 · campaign-link 16/16 · officers 15/15 — all byte-identical; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14/14; diag-classic paints nonBlank **346**; 0 pageerrors throughout). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: B4 distinct arm roles** (artillery canister/long-range; cavalry scout/flank/screen/raid — design drafted: the `ARM`-melee table is a dangling hook to fill; bullrun already fields Griffin/Ricketts as `art` + Stuart as `cav`; the Cannon-Corps→field-battery bridge [A1 currently re-arms inf only]; the cav-raid↔B-3-train tie) · B5 difficulty/realism presets · B6 the CS-player "command either side" mode (fork #10).

## D67 — PHASE B-4 · DISTINCT ARM ROLES (artillery canister + battery doctrine; cavalry scout/flank/screen/raid; the ARM melee table; the Cannon-Corps→battery bridge) + the BASE-ARM byte-identity fix + First Bull Run DEFAULTS TO FOG ON — [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-15)
The 4th V1-CHECKLIST Phase-B item (D61). Artillery + cavalry get real ROLES on top of the existing arm typing. New module `src/tactical/T5-arms.js` (the whole layer) + guarded T0 seams (`__FIELD.arms` gate w/ sticky `_armsOff`; `fldMakeUnit` carries `role`; an art canister multiplier in `fldResolveFire`; the ARM melee read in `fldResolveMelee`; an arm-aware target bias in `fldAcquireTarget`; an arm-role dispatch in `fldAiUnit`; a per-tick `fldArmsStep` in `fldSimStep`; HUD/end-screen/2D/3D hooks) + the T2 bridge (`_fldArtProfile`) + `data/bullrun.json` (Stuart `role:"flank"`, `defaultFog:true`) + `tools/probe-arms.mjs`. Deliverable ≈**1640KB**.
- **ARTILLERY:** `fldArtFireMult` — CANISTER (≤`CANISTER_R`=150yd) a damage spike (`CANISTER_MULT`=2.7) murderous in the open, sharply attenuated by cover (`CANISTER_COVER_K`/floor — works/woods defeat the balls); beyond, a softening long-range BOMBARDMENT (`LONG_MULT`=0.5, suppresses more than kills). `ARM.art`=0.35 melee → overrun. **The battery doctrine `fldAiArtillery` is ASYMMETRIC by role:** a DEFENDING battery is sited safe (fires from outside the ring on its own side; displaces early at `BATTERY_DISPLACE_R`=200), an ATTACKING battery pushes FORWARD to a canister post (`BATTERY_FWD_FRAC`) and bolts only at point-blank (`BATTERY_OVERRUN_R`=95) — so it CAN be overrun (Griffin/Ricketts, whose loss broke the Union attack). Never charges.
- **CAVALRY:** `fldAiCavalry` dispatches on `u.role` (default flank): **scout** (range wide to lift fog, avoid a stronger enemy), **flank** (a DEFENDING flanker is a leashed mobile reserve in the threatened ring; an ATTACKING flanker rides the open wing; charges a catchable disordered line — `CAV_CHARGE`=1.4 shock / `CAV_BRACE`=0.9 vs a steady braced line), **screen** (interpose between the enemy and the objective), **raid** (make for the ENEMY ammunition train and drain its reserve — `fldArmsStep`, the B-3 tie). Weak carbine — cavalry decide by mobility, not the firefight.
- **THE CANNON-CORPS → BATTERY BRIDGE:** `_fldArtProfile(C)` maps the player's dominant bought battery type (`C.artillery.batteries` × `data/artillery.json`) to the field battery's reach / per-shot power / canister strength, anchored at the Napoleon (no investment → null → nominal, balanced like the A1 strength anchor). "Build a Napoleon park → murderous canister; build Whitworths → long-range counter-battery with NO close spike." Applied in `fldCampaignConditionUnit` (the art branch; previously inf-only). Order-independent dominant-gun pick (sorted keys). **Reachable only via the campaign First-Bull-Run route this milestone (procedural/skirmish OOBs are inf-only — logged as a Phase-C follow-up).**
- **GATE + DETERMINISM:** fully behind `__FIELD.arms` (default ON live); the 8 baseline probes set sticky `_armsOff` → no canister/role-AI/raid, the ARM read falls back (see below) → byte-identical. No RNG in the role AI (deterministic; the fire/melee `fldRng` stream order unchanged).
- **THE BASE-ARM BYTE-IDENTITY BUG (caught in vetting, NOT by the design):** the B-4 design claimed `ARM` "is referenced but never defined → all arms melee at 1.0." **WRONG** — the FROZEN base engine defines `const ARM={ inf:{melee:1.00}, cav:{melee:1.05}, art:{melee:0.40}, … }` at `build/base.html:634`, and the build concatenates base+src, so `fldResolveMelee` was reading those REAL values. My first refactor dropped them to 1.0 when arms is off, shifting the arms-OFF balance (the bullrun probe missed it — it asserts behaviours, not the 8-seed win-count). **FIX:** arms-OFF `fldResolveMelee` now falls back to the BASE `ARM` table (only arms-ON uses the new FLDA values). Verified against the COMMITTED build: bare & logistics both **CS 5/8** byte-identical. A new probe step (`arms-OFF bullrun == committed 5/8`) locks this class.
- **THE STACKED-BALANCE FORK → FIRST BULL RUN DEFAULTS TO FOG ON (surfaced to Aaron, his call — D61-R1):** the per-layer probes each isolate the others, so the STACKED live config (officers+logistics+arms) was never measured. It is **Union-favoured in clear weather** — the COMMITTED D66 build is already **CS 3/8 fog-OFF** (a pre-existing miss), and B-4's arms layer dragged it to 0/8. Fog-ON is **CS 8/8** ("fog aids the defender" intact). A human (who commands the US attacker) is unaffected — it only skews the AI-vs-AI/auto-resolve diagnostic, which D64 wanted CS-favoured. **Aaron chose: make Bull Run default fog ON** (the historically faithful battle — smoke, broken terrain, green troops — where fog aids the defender → the Confederate victory). Implemented via `scenData.defaultFog` + a fog PRECEDENCE (explicit `opts.fog` > explicit `G.settings.tacticalFog` > scenario default), so only UNSET fog flips; the probes that pin fog stay byte-identical. Live stacked config → **CS 8/8**. (The pre-existing fog-OFF stacked interaction remains a possible future re-tune; fog-ON is now the faithful default.)
- **Balance A/B (8-seed Bull Run AI-vs-AI, CS=defender; logged):** bare 5/8 · logistics(arms-off) 5/8 [byte-identical] · arms-only fog-OFF **7/8** (CS-favoured, US breaks 1/8) · officers-only 7/8 · **LIVE stacked default (fog ON) 8/8** · the diagnostic that corrected my two wrong hypotheses: the lever was NOT artillery fire or cavalry but the battery doctrine over-protecting the US guns (a forward, exposed, pressured battery is balance-neutral; a safe rear-bombarding one is US-favouring).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (31 agents — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders × 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 2 distinct confirmed (deduped from 7) + 6 critic gaps, ALL FIXED:** **(HIGH)** the 3D arm meshes were built once at init, before Griffin/Ricketts/Stuart (all REINFORCEMENTS) detrained → invisible guns/horses in the default 3D Bull Run → rebuild `fld3dBuildArms` in `fldReinforceSpawn`; **(MED)** `fldArmsHudSelected`'s battery range-band scanned enemies with no `fldVisible` gate → leaked a hidden enemy's proximity under fog → fog-gated like the AI scanners; [critic gaps] no 3D render coverage → a stubbed-THREE build assertion; no arms-ON-pure-inf == arms-OFF assertion → added; reduceMotion untested → a recording-ctx assertion (no flash/cone/trail when reduced); `fldCavRaid` dispatch untested → added; `_fldArtProfile` key-order tie-break → sorted + a probe; art/cav-roles-only-in-bullrun1 → documented (Phase-C follow-up).
- **WCAG 2.2 AA (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** clean — all 8 new HUD/end-screen colour pairs pass (10:1+ on the dark field panel; the end-card border 3.03:1 ≥ 3:1, consistent with D66); decorative gun/trooper sprite colours left (CVD-safe shapes). No fix needed.
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1640KB) → **probe-arms 23/23, 0 pageerrors** (build/off-inert; ARM table; end-to-end overrun; canister open/cover/long; battery asymmetric doctrine; the 4 cavalry roles + the raid-train tie; target bias; the Cannon-Corps bridge; 3D arm meshes on reinforcement; arms-ON-inf & arms-OFF-bullrun byte-identity; reduceMotion; tie-break; **the fog-default + stacked CS 8/8**; the fog-OFF CS-favoured band; sandbox no-op; no Classic contamination) → **full no-regression GREEN** (field 13/13 · bullrun 15/15 · fog 13/13 · autopause 13/13 · ai 15/15 · campaign-link 16/16 · officers 15/15 · logistics 14/14 — all byte-identical; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14/14; diag-classic nonBlank **346**; strategic spot-check desk/economy/victory green; 0 pageerrors). Committed + pushed after full vetting. **NEXT: B5 difficulty/realism presets** (+ the engineering-slider directive, memory `civilwar-directive-tactical-engineering-sliders`) · B6 the CS-player "command either side" mode (fork #10).

## D68 — RUN-K DESIGN Q&A #3: a 30-question scope/gameplay sweep (10 rounds × 3) — refinements to the V1 roadmap — [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-15)
Aaron ran a 10-round popup sweep (3 questions/round, recommendation = option 1) to clarify/refine/expand/contract scope. He confirmed popups are useful **when each question is a genuine fork that changes the build** — keep them surgical, not a ritual (I self-police: ~3 questions only at a real fork; flag the complexity cost on any scope-expanding answer). **Net deltas to the locked V1-CHECKLIST/D54/D61 (mostly EXPAND; a few CONTRACT; the rest confirm current direction):**
- **EXPANSIONS:** (1) **Expansive v1** — fold the come-to-life media + loot/survival into core, do NOT defer to a "v2". (2) **Zoomable battle scale** — brigades expand into regiments on zoom (a new tactical-engine requirement beyond the current brigade abstraction). (3) **Wide-open alt-history sandbox** — more latitude than D54's "consensus-favoured" (CSA-victory / foreign-war paths allowed); reconcile with the teaching mission via deep citations + honest framing + the "your war vs history" tracker (a CSA-win path is taught with its real implications, never glorified). (4) **Even-deeper citations** — footnote-level sources, a bibliography, scholar attributions. (5) **Custom-battle builder EARLY** (tools-first, ahead of some breadth). (6) **Many granular difficulty sliders** (per-lever, beyond the 2-axis B-5 plan). (7) **Heavy embedded media** (bundle PD imagery/footage into the deliverable — flag: pushes past the lean single file; plan Phase H to compress/tier so portability survives). (8) **Rich adaptive musical score** (beyond default-off tunes). (9) **Loot/survival → a CORE PILLAR** (always-on progression + journey mode, not a deferred optional; keep preset-gateable down for the pure-historian).
- **CONTRACTIONS:** (10) **"hex and classic are the same thing"** — do NOT build a separate new co-equal hex engine; the existing FROZEN Classic hex IS the turn-based mode, and modern scenarios reach it via the bridge ("To the Field (Classic)", largely done in Phase A). Phase D shrinks from "new engine" to "make modern battles selectable in Classic." (11) **AA essentials only** — core WCAG-AA kept as-built, but DROP the 4 specialized a11y modes from v1 (contracts E3). (12) **Tooltips-only onboarding** — drop the layered tutorial/codex (contracts E2).
- **CONFIRMED (no change):** President+commander hybrid fantasy; line/column/skirmish+facing; layered-but-readable morale; direct drag-to-command; smarter-not-cheating AI + preset handicaps; officers w/ command radius+traits+can-be-hit; the current economy/diplomacy/politics depth (refine, don't expand to full sub-games); ambient teaching that confers mastery; Eastern-marquee battles first; both full-war campaign + standalone battles; period engraving/broadsheet art; saves (localStorage+slots+export); data-driven+shareable modding; alt-history-divergence replay; both snackable + long sessions; sober museum-grade anti-Lost-Cause tone. **Action:** these refine the V1-CHECKLIST (Phase F women-in-the-war + tactical-engineering ideas already logged D67-adjacent); the EXPANSIONS/CONTRACTIONS will be threaded into the relevant phases as they're built.

## D69 — PHASE B-5 DESIGN CLEARED (difficulty/realism presets) + the engineering/roadmap forks — [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-15)
