## D92 — ROSTER HISTORY-ACCURACY HARDENING (all 9 shipped battles) + the accurate-inputs principle — [OPUS, Aaron-directed] (2026-06-21)
Aaron asked whether the full Chattanooga-grade rigor (citation-grade research + adversarial verify, casualty-direction guards, balance sweep) had been applied to the battles already built. It had NOT for the 7 pre-Opus battles (the Codex/early-built C1 Eastern marquee + Shiloh + Bull Run); only Vicksburg + Chickamauga (Opus, bug-hunted) had the adversarial history pass.
- **Adversarial audit (Workflow, 9 Opus historians + critic + a consolidated casualty-direction sweep `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs`):** found **15 HIGH-severity wrong facts shipped under "Verified" stamps** — overwhelmingly the **rank-at-the-battle** class (a later/posthumous/backdated promotion applied to the battle date), plus wrong-division (the Vicksburg "Hebert" class) and a **dead officer commanding a battery**. ALL FIXED, each annotated in-file:
  - **Malvern Hill (4):** Hunt Brig.Gen.→**Col.** (file self-contradicted, calling him Col. elsewhere); Jackson Lt.Gen.→**Maj.Gen.** (no CSA Lt.Gen. grade until Oct 1862 — the Hood-at-Chickamauga anachronism); Porter Maj.Gen.→**Brig.Gen.** (MG dated Jul 4, 3 days after); Hooker Brig.Gen.→**Maj.Gen.** (under-ranked).
  - **Chancellorsville (4):** Rodes Maj.Gen.→**Brig.Gen.** (MG conferred after, for this flank attack); Berry **III Corps** not II; Paxton's Stonewall Brigade re-attached to **Colston's division** not A.P. Hill's (Hebert-class); Fairview battery **Capt. Hazzard (DEAD, d. Aug 1862) → Capt. Clermont L. Best**.
  - **Shiloh (3):** Breckinridge Maj.Gen.→**Brig.Gen.** (MG Apr 14, 8 days after); Bragg led the **RIGHT** wing not the left (contradicted its own teaching card); W.H.L. Wallace died **Apr 10** not May 10.
  - **Gettysburg (3):** Doubleday & Early Brig.Gen.→**Maj.Gen.** (both under-ranked); Stannard's Vermont Bde **I Corps** not III.
  - **Vicksburg (1):** Martin L. Smith Maj.Gen.→**Brig.Gen.** (×3 fields; MG dated Nov 1863, 4 months AFTER the surrender).
  - Plus ~12 medium/low (Antietam Benjamin 1st-Lt + **4 not 6 guns** + Graham Capt; Shiloh Wood-as-reserve→**Chalmers's evening assault** / Taylor-on-Battery-A→**Peter P. Wood** / Trabue→Robert P., infantry not artillery; Bull Run Pelham's-battery→**Alburtis's** / Elzey 13th VA + 1st Md Infantry; Fredericksburg Ransom echelon reframe; Gettysburg Archer captured at **Willoughby Run** not the Railroad Cut; Chickamauga Negley **court of inquiry** not court-martial + Cheatham's Preston Smith brigade added).
  - **SURFACED, deliberately NOT auto-fixed (genuine source conflict, per Aaron's rule):** Bull Run **Heintzelman** (Col. vs Brig. Gen. — regular-vs-volunteer commission conflict) and Antietam **Mansfield** (his Maj.Gen.-of-volunteers dated Jul 18 1862 predates the battle — the data's "Maj. Gen." is defensible; the auditor's downgrade is contestable). Left as-is for a future editor.
- **THE LOCKED PRINCIPLE (Aaron, verbatim during the pass):** "I want skill and gameplay and weapon type etc to impact outcomes — that's the priority over staying absolutely accurate to history. I don't want the no-lost-cause to be over-interpreted." Outcomes EMERGE from skill + weapon type + terrain + tactics via the D74 universal model. History enters ONLY as the **default equipment** (accurate soldier/gun counts, weapons, terrain, doctrine) so the **probable** result lands near the historical one *because the inputs are true* — **NEVER an output gate forcing a casualty direction or winner.** So we **DROPPED** the planned "fix Antietam so the CS doesn't out-bleed the Union" balance refight and the hard historical-direction probe gates; `sweep-all-battles.mjs` stays a DIAGNOSTIC. The only casualty guards kept/added are **system validations** (cover reduces casualties, rifled out-ranges smoothbore, more guns = more fire) that keep the game LEGIBLE (a player can read the visible OOB and forecast probable odds + casualty %). A teaching-text-vs-sim divergence is the intended "your war vs history," not a defect. (Full principle: memory `civilwar-roster-accuracy-principle`.)
- **Verification:** ALL edits are labels/notes only EXCEPT one accurate gun-count (Antietam Benjamin 6→4) + one unit re-identification keeping stats (Shiloh Wood→Chalmers). `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; full re-vet GREEN — all 9 battle probes (bullrun 15 · malvern 24 · antietam 16 · fredericksburg 22 · chancellorsville 24 · gettysburg 16 · shiloh 29 · vicksburg 18 · chickamauga 18) + roster 8 + custom-builder 9, **each battle's own balance assertions still green** (outcomes byte-preserved), diag-classic `nonBlank:346`, 0 pageerrors; broad tactical-systems suite + boot/t1 green. New `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs` consolidated casualty-direction diagnostic.
- **D92-verify (2026-06-21, resumed session after an API-error hang):** the D92 work was on disk but uncommitted when the prior session died on a 529. Before committing, an **independent adversarial re-verification** (Workflow: 1 Opus historian per battle + critic, re-run for the 2 that 529'd) checked every asserted correction against 2+ sources to catch a "fix" that was itself wrong. The 6/9 + 2 re-run + chancellorsville came back GO; it found **4 more items, ALL FIXED before commit:** (1) **Bull Run** — the D92 `cs_elzey` gloss "(Elzey's own regiment)" was attached to the 10th/13th Virginia, but Elzey's own regiment was the **1st Maryland** (he had colonel'd it); the 13th Va. was A. P. Hill's, the 10th Gibbons's — gloss moved to the 1st Maryland (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). (2) **Shiloh** — `us_buell_ammen` was "Brig. Gen." but Jacob **Ammen was a COLONEL** (24th Ohio) at Shiloh; his BG dated Jul 16 1862, after the battle (the anachronistic-rank class, *missed* by D92) → Col. (3) **Antietam** — `us_battery_b` (Gibbon's Battery B, 4th U.S.) was tagged `rifled` but was **six 12-pdr Napoleons (smoothbore)** — its own note already said "double canister," the smoothbore signature; corrected `rifled→smooth` (an accurate-weapon input per the D92-locked principle; the antietam probe stayed 16/16 so the Cornfield outcome is byte-preserved — outcome-neutral). (4) **Malvern Hill** — D92 had *over-promoted* `us_hooker` BG→Maj. Gen. by his May-5-1862 date-of-rank, but Hooker's MG commission was **issued Jul 26 1862 (after the battle) and backdated**; the canonical Seven Days OOB lists him **BG**, exactly as the file (correctly) keeps Porter/Couch/Kearny — reverted to Brig. Gen. for internal consistency (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). Net beyond the original D92: 3 label fixes + 1 outcome-neutral weapon-tag fix. Re-vet GREEN (full battle + roster + custom + systems suite + diag-classic `nonBlank:346` + boot/t1, 0 pageerrors). THEN committed + pushed.

## D93 — "THE SOLDIER'S STORY" character/narrative pillar — captured + scheduled — [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + directive, 2026-06-21)
Aaron's vision for an individual character/narrative layer, modeled on EA-Sports rosters. Captured here + memory `civilwar-soldiers-story-pillar`; **scheduled AFTER the C+E roadmap** (his choice) — NOT built now.
- **Spec:** a complete **prosopographical database** — *every identifiable individual* in the modeled battles, each with **bio, stats/ratings, character history, portrait (procedural now / PD photo Phase H), and team (army→corps→division→brigade→regiment→company)** — plus a **"play as anyone" whole-war mode**: pick any identified person, choose **when + where to start**, proceed from their **REAL rank and position** at that moment, then play forward into alt-history.
- **Aaron's 3 scoping answers (AskUserQuestion):** (1) granularity = **"every named individual found"** (exhaustive); (2) sequencing = **AFTER C+E** (finish Chattanooga + C3 USCT + the E strategic arc first); (3) shape = **unified journey-mode pillar** (merge with the D91 loot/survival journey mode; design the playthrough + interpersonal/**romance** threads as one deliberate pillar).
- **Build order (bottom-up — the data is the substrate):** (1) granular OOB + per-person/regiment **detail cards** (DATA, reuses teaching cards, NO tactical-engine change — brigades stay one marker per the D68 zoom-deferral); (2) codex **person/unit axis** (D34.3, Phase E/S4); (3) **individual playthrough mode** (the thread connecting tactical↔strategic↔narrative; = the D91 journey mode + a narrative spine); (4) **interpersonal/romance** (women-in-the-war / USCT / immigrant hooks; period-honest, anti-Lost-Cause). The real SYSTEM work is the **career/trajectory model** (each person's whole-war path) + the **start-anywhere engine**; the roster is large-but-bounded content.
- **Hard dependency:** accurate rank+position+unit per person — **the D92 roster hardening is the first roster data** and a prerequisite for "start from real rank."

## D94 — THE RATING SYSTEM (the OVR / "Madden layer") — designed + build authorized — [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + 3 directives, 2026-06-21)
A Madden-style **1–100 OVR + badges/abilities** for soldiers, officers, and brigades, the substrate for the D93 Soldier's Story. Full design law in **`RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`** (a 3-lens design Workflow: B sim-accurate-input spine + C prosopography data substrate + A Madden Star/Superstar/X-Factor feel, judged + synthesized; verified against the live engine).
- **The keystone (honors D74/D92):** ratings FULLY decide casualties + winners — but *through the inputs, not by editing the scoreboard*. A documented persona is *derived* into true attributes that *seed* the levers the engine already reads (`xp`, `quality`→`cmdBonus`, `weapon`, `radius`, `fate`, `cohesion`, bounded `sev.*`) ONCE at build/preset-apply, then the normal combat model runs on them → the strong unit dominates *emergently* (and can still be out-played). The ONLY forbidden act (the "output wall", build-gate-asserted) is a handler writing `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/victory/`tgt.men` or out-of-band `sev.*` **directly** at resolution time (the scripted "higher rating ⇒ auto-win" hack — it would make the sim a cutscene and kill the teaching). One spine, anchored at 64 → a neutral unit is byte-identical to Classic.
- **Unifies, does not duplicate:** the officer OVR **is** `_cmdGenRating` (`0.55*skill+0.45*reputation`); reuses `commandLeadership` (the 42–88 bridge), `_cmdLeadWord`, `_cmdTraitBar`; persona inserts only at the FRONT (persona→`gen.skill`). No parallel rating, no second bridge.
- **Aaron's 4 locked directives (AskUserQuestion + follow-ups):** (1) **BUILD THE FULL SYSTEM NOW** — R-0→R-4 reprioritized *ahead of* Chattanooga (pulls D93 forward); (2) **X-Factor feel = DRAMATIC Madden surge** (visible glow + announce + strong swing, still hard-capped under `CMD_BONUS_CAP 0.9` — the cap, not the feel, is the wall); (3) **negatives = VERIFIED + plainly named** (Bragg "Piecemeal", McClellan "The Slows" — anti-Lost-Cause rigor applies to flaws too, ≥2 sources); (4) **tier scale = A–F report-card** (A+ ≥90 "Legendary" club, then A/B/C/D/F — NO gaming "S"; neutral 64 = C).
- **"Integrated in ALL layers" (Aaron directive):** the OVR surfaces + bites in the strategic President's Desk (appointment pool/cabinet/command OVR+grade+badges), the War-Effort army-quality readouts, **auto-resolve** (a capped `_cmdBadgeEdge` on the margin), **Classic hex** (OVR-derived quality via the `86-battle-conditioning` ±12% anchor, base unedited), the **real-time tactical** field (the full badge/X-Factor seams), **campaign progression** (reputation→OVR dev-traits), the Custom Battle Builder, and the D93 journey mode — all three battle modes read the SAME rating-derived inputs so they stay substitutable (the D62 bridge property). The rating never forces an outcome in any layer.
- **Build increments (each byte-identical-when-inactive, fully vetted + pushed):** R-0 data spine (`data/ratings.json` + `src/tactical/T14-ratings.js` pure fns + `tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, no combat seam) · R-1 officer derivation→pipe · R-2 OVR read-out UI (A–F, WCAG/CVD triple-encode) · R-3 badge engine + global per-lever stacking cap + all-layers wiring · R-4 X-Factors (deterministic seed-replay no-fudge gate) · R-5 D93 scale-out (lazy per-person materialization) · R-6 negative-badge sweep + dev-traits. Calibration oracle: the derivation table is regression-locked against the 9 shipped scenarios' authored `quality`/`xp` before any mass generation. (Reversible; design law in `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`.)
- **D94-elicitation (Aaron, 10 rounds × 3 AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-21) — `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md` §15 has the full 30 answers.** The system grew substantially (Aaron chose comprehensively, mostly all-of-the-above): **~15 attributes** (the 10 + initiative/logistics/engineering/cavalry/artillery), shared-set/weighted-by-level, **own-visible/enemy-fuzzy**; badge kinds span ALL types at every rung (Star drill/terrain/arm/veteran · Superstar auras/tactics/reputation/logistics · X-Factor historical/surge/heroic/doomed); negatives ALL kinds (command/vice/unit/political); general strategic skills (maneuver/logistics/political/coordination); brigade identity (legend/ethnic/veteran/hard-luck). **NEW subsystems:** a between-battle **camp loop** — drilling-as-practice (focus-or-delegate, concordant battlefield bonuses) + **simmable scouting** (tiered by cavalry/recon) + **progression** (combat-XP + drilling + hidden potential ceiling + attrition decline). The **Army GM franchise layer** — a **war-wide free-agency pool** (alt-history dream-teams, balanced by a **symmetric AI GM** + difficulty scaling + clout cost + historical anchors), **all promotion paths** (merit/capital/seniority/field-brevet), killed-officer permadeath, and a **FULL multi-currency economy** (political capital + seniority/manpower + supply) earned from all sources, pressured by factional demands + event shocks. **Matchups:** dual **Attack/Defend OVR** + a full pre-battle matchup screen; emergent counters surfaced as advice. **UI:** period "Army Register" broadsheet roster; in-battle badges via HUD chips + X-Factor banner/glow + floating proc text + marker glyph; initials/rank portraits now. **Data:** full prosopography target, strict 2+ source provenance. **Ship order:** OVR+badges-in-battle first.
- **D94-softcap (the one reconciliation, decide-&-log):** Aaron chose "**soften the cap for power-fantasy**" over "keep the hard wall." Reconciled to honor BOTH it and the D74/D92 non-negotiable: the **OUTPUT wall stays absolute** (no rating ever read when a casualty/winner is computed — architectural invariant, build-gate-asserted), while the **INPUT caps soften and scale with the existing B-5 realism slider** — **Arcade = generous/dramatic dream-team power-fantasy, Balanced = moderate, Historian = the tight historical wall** (the citation-grade teaching mode). The dramatic feel comes from a generous *input* cap, never an absent *output* wall; no outcome is ever scripted at any setting. (Surfaced to Aaron; proceeding with the slider-scaled version unless he prefers a flat higher ceiling at all difficulties.)
- **D94-forks (Aaron, 8 resolved via 2 AskUserQuestion rounds, 2026-06-21):** (1) **soft-cap = realism-slider-scaled CONFIRMED** (Arcade generous / Balanced moderate / Historian tight — the §15.1 reconciliation stands). (2) **Legendary A+ (≥90) = PURE MERIT, no club cap** — whoever's Verified attributes earn ≥90 is A+; anti-Lost-Cause is guarded by the citation-grade attribute *sourcing*, NOT by capping the club size (consistent with no-output-gate). DROP the planned "not >60% one side" balance gate. (3) **Political-general bind = SOFTER flavor cost** — a political-capital surcharge + a flavor note, NO election-support mechanic (simpler than the "real election cost" rec). (4) **`cohesion` = a NEW REQUIRED authored field** — author it on units across scenarios (engine keeps a derive-from-`xp` fallback only as a safety net so un-migrated data stays byte-identical). (5) **Reputation→OVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign now** (wins/losses visibly move a general's OVR via `cmdOnResolve`). (6) **GM transfers/commissions (the war-wide free-agency pool) = available FROM THE START** (full depth-chart control turn 1). (7) **The 2 surfaced rank disputes (Bull Run Heintzelman, Antietam Mansfield) = resolve by the PREVAILING source + annotate the dispute** (overnight run: a quick verify — note Heintzelman was appointed Brig. Gen. of vols May 17 1861 so the prevailing grade at First Bull Run is Brig. Gen.; Mansfield's Maj. Gen. of vols dated Jul 18 1862 predates Antietam so Maj. Gen. stands — confirm 2+ sources, apply, annotate). (8) **Overnight bar = BALANCE breadth + polish** (many milestones, each above-and-beyond, no gold-plating one at the cost of three). Also re-confirmed from the elicitation: negatives Verified+plainly-named, A-F scale, dual Attack/Defend OVR, full multi-currency economy.

## D95 — RATING SYSTEM **R-1**: officer derivation into the existing command + field pipes (the persona becomes the source of truth) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first wiring increment of the D94 rating system (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §9 R-1). The documented persona now SEEDS the levers the two pipes already read — **strategic** `gen.skill` and **tactical** officer `quality`/`radius`/`fate` — with the no-fudge keystone intact (the persona only sets inputs at build/make time; nothing is read at casualty/winner/rout time) and every unrated/un-opted entity **byte-identical**.
- **Strategic leg (`src/35-command.js`):** new `_cmdGenPersona(gen)` + `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen)`; `_cmdGenRating` now derives `skill` from the linked persona (`command/tactical/discipline` → `fldOfficerSkillSeed`) instead of reading the static `gen.skill`. **Calibration oracle (strategic):** the 9 personas are authored so `round(0.45*command+0.35*tactical+0.20*discipline) === the Verified gen.skill EXACTLY` (FP-boundary-safe; min distance from the round-half boundary 0.2) → `commandLeadership`/auto-resolve/conditioning stay **byte-identical** and the appoint-pool words still match history, while the persona is now the source. `cmdActiveTraits.skill` + the Command-desk Skill bar also route through `_cmdEffectiveSkill` (one source of truth; the bug-hunt critic's single-source-of-truth fix — byte-identical today, closes the future-drift footgun). Unrated generals keep authored `gen.skill`.
- **Tactical leg (`src/tactical/T3-officers.js`):** new `fldOfficerPersona(o)` + `fldMakeOfficer` derives `quality` (`fldPersonaQuality`, calibrated to reproduce the authored field quality within ≤0.005 — the R-0 oracle, so a rated aura shifts only slightly), `radius` (authored echelon range + a small charisma nudge, clamped 160–290), and `fate` (the persona's durability multiplier, which matches the authored scenario fate for the Bull Run cast). **EXPLICIT `pid` opt-in, NO `id` fallback** — the bug-hunt-class fix for a real **cross-scenario id collision**: leader ids are reused across battles (`ld_jackson` is the 1861 brigadier at Bull Run but a corps commander at Antietam/Chancellorsville), so an `id`-match would leak the wrong persona; a leader derives ONLY when it names a persona via `pid`. The 7 Bull Run leaders are opted in (`data/bullrun.json`); every other scenario's leaders have no `pid` → byte-identical until their personas are authored.
- **`data/ratings.json` — NEW `generalPersonas` map** (9 strategic army-commander personas keyed by the `data/generals.json` id): **CS** Lee, Jackson, A.S. Johnston, Bragg, Longstreet · **US** McClellan, Grant, Burnside, Meade — the principal commanders of the 9 D92-hardened battles (Bull Run is covered by the field cast). A SEPARATE record from the Bull Run FIELD cast (war-long army commander vs the 1861 brigade officer); R-5 unifies them into one prosopography person. The documented character + the named negatives (McClellan `the_slows`, Burnside `rigid_plan`, Bragg `piecemeal`) are Verified with real sources (Sears 1988, Marvel 1991, Robertson 1997, Hess 2016, Wert 1993, Chernow 2017, McPherson 1988, …); the attribute VECTOR is Inferred designer calibration anchored to each Verified `gen.skill`; `aggression` tracks the documented temperament and is EXCLUDED from the headline OVR (anti-Lost-Cause).

(Reversible; design law RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §5/§6/§9.)

## D96 — RATING SYSTEM **R-2**: the OVR read-out UI (Command desk grades + tactical HUD brigade OVR) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The display increment (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §9 R-2 + §3 bands + §10 the WCAG/CVD badge UI). **PURE DISPLAY — no sim change, byte-identical** (the full no-regression suite confirms all 9 battles byte-identical). The rating numbers the R-1 spine already produces are now surfaced + graded A–F.

- **WCAG 2.2 AA + CVD-safe (the §10 mandate):** every surface is **triple-encoded — number + letter-grade + word in the high-contrast `--parch` text; colour is DECORATIVE only** (aria-hidden left-border stripes / dots), so meaning never rides colour alone (deuteranopia/protanopia safe). `wcag-auditor` (Sonnet) verified all three new surfaces PASS AA. Two pre-existing secondary labels (the "In command" status label + the "generals at your call" header) used `--rule #8a7350` (3.25:1 on the real desk ground — a long-standing sub-AA) and were lifted to **#b3925e (5.0:1 worst-case, measured against the actual `.sheet` radial gradient `#26200f→#161009` + the 4% light overlay, NOT pure black)** — the R-2 adversarial bug-hunt caught that the wcag-auditor's first fix (#8d7551) had been computed against pure black and still failed AA on the real lighter ground.
- **Vetting:** GATE OK; `probe-ratings` **14/14** + `probe-command` **16/16** (new R-2 UI assertion steps: the HUD line + the desk card/pool grades are triple-encoded); FULL no-regression GREEN (28 probes — all 9 battles + the systems suite byte-identical); diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (3 Opus lenses × default-refute verify + a completeness critic): **2 confirmed** (the false-AA contrast claim — FIXED to a genuinely-AA, honestly-measured colour) + **2 critic findings** (a `/* */` audit comment was glued INSIDE an inline-style string and shipped into the rendered DOM → moved outside the JS string, DOM-leak signature now 0; and `gr.word`/`g.word` were interpolated unescaped while `gr.letter` was escaped → escaped at all sites for defense-in-depth, byte-identical today). ## D97 — RATING SYSTEM **R-3**: the badge engine (the first rating→combat seam) + the no-fudge build-gate — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first place a rating actually TOUCHES combat (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §4/§6/§9 R-3). A guarded one-token factor seeds the levers the engine already reads; the no-fudge OUTPUT wall is now enforced **structurally** by the build. **Byte-identical when off** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles produce identical deterministic results on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build).
- **`fldBadgeFactor(u, lever)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** the guarded MULTIPLICATIVE one-token factor — IDENTITY 1.0 when `__FIELD.badges` is off OR the unit carries no matching badge (mirrors the `(u.cmdBonus||0)` no-op). It sums the unit's badges' signed `mag`s for a lever, gates each by its trigger (`_fldBadgeTrig`: always/march/in_woods/arm_cav/arm_art; others default on, an R-4 refinement), then CLAMPS the summed delta to the realism-scaled per-unit per-lever cap (`fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"badgeLever")` — arcade .16 / balanced .10 / historian .06, D94-softcap). Negatives are DAMPERS (factor<1, ≥1−cap), never enemy buffs. Pure read; returns a factor, never writes state. Plus `fldUnitCohesion(u)` ((cohesion−50)/50, clamped [−1,1]; **0 when cohesion unauthored** → byte-identical — the rally term defaults neutral, NOT xp-derived, since an xp-derived default would shift the rally of every xp≠2 unit).
- **Four guarded seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** fire (`fldResolveFire` `power *= fldBadgeFactor(u,"fire")`), rally (`fldMoraleStep` `rally = (1 + xp*.12*vet + .06*cohesion*vet) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"rally")`), melee (`fldResolveMelee` atk/def), speed (`fldMoveFactor` `(u._spdMul||1) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"speed")` — `_spdMul` reserved for the R-4 X-Factor surge). All identity when off. The `__FIELD.badges` gate (default ON, `_badgesOff` hook) + `__FIELD.realismTier` (set in `fldPresetsApply`, default balanced) added.
- **Badge data (`data/ratings.json`):** each of the 25 badgeDefs now carries `fldLever` (fire/rally/speed/melee, or `none` for officer-aura / auto-resolve-edge / canister / sight effects deferred to R-4/§7.5) + a signed `mag`. Ships the Star/Superstar positives + the Verified named negatives with real tactical bite: McClellan **The Slows** (speed −0.08), Bragg **Piecemeal** (rally −0.05), Burnside **Rigid Plan** (fire −0.05), **Green Levies** (rally −0.08), **Powder-Shy** (rally −0.05); positives marksman/woods_fighter (fire), disciplined/blooded/beloved/stonewall (rally), hardy_marcher/horseman (speed). Badges are NOT yet assigned to shipped scenario rosters (that is the R-6 sweep) → every battle stays byte-identical.
- **The NO-FUDGE OUTPUT WALL, build-gate-asserted (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4d):** the rating module (`tactical/T14-ratings.js`) is scanned at build for any write to `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/`.victory`/`.men`/`sev.*` — dot AND bracket notation (the bracket variants close the bug-hunt's computed-member bypass) — and the build FAILS (exit 5) if found. Verified firing on planted `u.men=0`, `u["men"]=0`, and `F.sev["attrition"]=2` writes; clean build prints `GATE OK · … · no-fudge ✓`. The combat modules legitimately write these; the wall scopes to the rating/badge module, which may only seed inputs + return factors.
- **Vetting — NOTE the environmental deviation:** GATE OK (incl. the new no-fudge gate). The standard `load`-based probe suite was **environmentally BLOCKED** this session: headless Chrome's `load` event never fires for the game page (the THREE-CDN `<script>` stalls in headless intermittently; it broke the committed-green R-2 build identically; a trivial page fires `load` in 73ms; `domcontentloaded` loads everything incl. THREE in ~1.5s). Root contributors: (a) the single-threaded `python -m http.server` chokes on the page's ~170 local asset requests (fixed by a **ThreadingHTTPServer**); (b) the THREE-CDN `load` stall (the documented gotcha). So R-3 was vetted via a **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness** (`.tmp/r3-verify.mjs`): it ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically (same seed) on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build and confirmed **IDENTICAL** casualties/winner/steps for all 10, plus the full badge-logic assertions (off=1, single=1.06, stack clamps to 1.10=1+cap, realism arc 1.16 > bal 1.10 > his 1.06, negatives 0.92, cohesion math), 0 pageerrors. This cross-build diff is a *stronger* byte-identity check than the standard probes. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (4 Opus lenses × refute-verify + critic): 2 confirmed (the gate-4d bracket bypass — FIXED by adding bracket regexes; a phantom `'sharpshooters'` key in the probe/T0 comment — FIXED) + 0 critic. Committed + pushed.
- **LESSON (probe harness, recurring — surface for the gotchas):** serve probes with a **ThreadingHTTPServer** (single-threaded chokes on the asset storm), and when headless `load` stalls on the THREE CDN, the resilient path is `waitUntil:'domcontentloaded'` (the documented gotcha) — the logic/sim probes don't need THREE. RECOMMENDED follow-up (next session, when the env is healthy OR as a harness fix): re-run the standard `load` suite to confirm green, and/or adopt a domcontentloaded+settle wait in the probe runner / vendor THREE locally so the suite is resilient. (Reversible; design law RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §4/§6/§9.)

## D98 — RATING SYSTEM **R-4**: the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" Madden surge, inside the no-fudge wall) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The dramatic increment (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §4/§6/§9 R-4, D94 fork-1 "DRAMATIC surge"). An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and SURGES on ONE channel, hard-capped — a visible, announced swing that provably can never breach the no-fudge wall. **Byte-identical when off / unassigned** (proven: a `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically on the R-4 build vs the committed R-3 build (HEAD dc9ba61) → **IDENTICAL** winner/US-cas/CS-cas/steps for all 10, 0 pageerrors).
- **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), tests its activation (`_fldXFactorInZone`: march_vigor=moving · his_offensive=moving/charging · ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging · last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) · usct_assault/mass_assault=charging · flanking=cav & charging) and, when in the zone, sets the surge on EXACTLY ONE channel (its declared lever): a **NON-speed** X-Factor (rally/melee/none) sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a **SPEED** X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT surge the command aura. One-shot ⚡ `fldAnnounce` + `fldScenarioBanner` on the rising edge (`_xfOn`); a marker glow (`_xfGlow`); deterministic decay (`_fldXfDecay`) toward identity out of zone. **NO RNG** → seed-replayable. A unit carrying no X-Factor is left wholly untouched (`_xf*`/`_spdMul` stay undefined) → byte-identical.
- **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** scales the unit's ALREADY-SUMMED command aura `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` — pushes the aura toward the **hard 0.9 wall, NEVER beyond**. A strict no-op unless an X-Factor is active (`_xfActive` undefined/≤1) → byte-identical. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (so the aura is summed first), gated on `__FIELD.badges` (NOT officers) so the cmdBonus surge and the `_spdMul` surge share ONE gate.
- **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` calls `fldXFactorStep(dt)` just before `fldOfficersStep` + the apply loop just after; `fldMoveFactor` clamps the **COMBINED** speed factor (the `_spdMul` surge × the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** so no stack can breach it (exactly 1 when no rating speed input → byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` pulse — a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries the meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font/tofu dependency), `reduceMotion`-honored, drawn for no shipped unit → byte-identical.
- **Data (`data/ratings.json`):** ADDED `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav, flanking trigger, fldLever none → surges via the capped cmdBonus only; 2 sources → Verified). The 7 X-Factors: foot_cavalry, rock_of_chickamauga, bayonet, earned_in_blood, grand_charge, first_with_the_most, the_slows. NOT assigned to any shipped scenario (the R-6 sweep) → byte-identical.
- **NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE (`tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, +2 steps → 17/17):** a deterministic seed-replay tags one CS sandbox brigade with foot_cavalry and runs it vs the untagged baseline (same seed): the surge **BITES** (it flipped a US win into a CS win) yet stays **bounded** (17.2% total-casualty delta — an input nudge, not a scripted result) and the **wall holds** (`maxCmd 0.47 < 0.9`). Plus synthetic asserts: speed X-Factor surges only `_spdMul` (no cmdBonus), non-speed surges cmdBonus capped at the wall, the combined-speed clamp binds at 1.30, negatives drag, realism-monotone amp, decay→1.
- **Vetting (env note — the `load` stall recurred intermittently):** GATE OK (no-fudge ✓); `probe-ratings` 17/17; the **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** (the authoritative X-Factor-off no-regression proof, `domcontentloaded` — independent of the flaky `load` event); the 9 battle probes + field + logistics + bootprobe passed via `load` (when it was momentarily healthy); `tactical-visuals` 10/10 scenes, 0 pe; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`. The systems probes (officers/command/presets/…) were `load`-stalled this session, but the byte-identity harness runs the full `fldSimStep`→`fldXFactorStep`→`fldOfficersStep` path (officers ON) for sandbox + all 9 battles and proves it byte-identical, covering their core concern. Re-confirm them next session once `load` is healthy (the durable fix — domcontentloaded+settle in the probe runner, or vendor THREE — remains a recommended small milestone).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (23 Opus agents: 6 diverse-lens finders × refute-verify + a completeness critic; 16 raw → 4 confirmed + 3 critic, **0 HIGH, all LATENT** [fire only at R-6 when badges are assigned to units; today byte-identical]). ALL 7 addressed: (1) speed double-count (foot_cavalry/the_slows hit both the static `fldBadgeFactor` and the `_spdMul` surge) → **combined-speed clamp [0.75,1.30] in `fldMoveFactor`**; (2) foot_cavalry got an undeclared cmdBonus surge → **gate the cmdBonus surge to NON-speed X-Factors only** (one channel per badge); (3) Star speed badges (hardy_marcher/horseman) stack with the surge → covered by the same combined clamp; (4) cmdBonus apply was officers-gated while `_spdMul` wasn't → **moved the apply to `fldSimStep`, gated on `badges`**; (5) `grand_charge` "dual" downside unimplemented → noted in data as an R-6 bounded-input-lever deferral (the engine delivers the bounded upside today); (6) ⚡ emoji canvas tofu risk → **vector-drawn bolt**; (7) `grand_charge` prov Verified-with-0-sources → downgraded to **Inferred**. Re-vetted after the fixes (probe-ratings 17/17 + byte-identity 10/10 still green).
- **DECIDED-&-LOGGED (incidental, pre-existing, out of R-4 scope):** the badge catalog has a **catalog-wide provenance gap** — several badgeDefs carry `prov:"Verified"` with <2 sources (R-0/R-3 convention): 0-source `rally`/`flank_march`/`massed_battery`/`feared`/`beloved`/`pontoon_master`/`grand_charge`[fixed→Inferred]; 1-source `foot_cavalry`/`rock_of_chickamauga`/`bayonet`/`earned_in_blood`/`the_slows`/`rigid_plan`/`reckless_valor`. This breaches the ≥2-source Verified rule but has **zero behavioral reach** (prov is display metadata; never read in combat). Fixed the clearest case (`grand_charge`, 0 sources). The proper fix — a citation **research+verify** workflow adding genuine 2nd sources per badge — belongs to the **R-6 content pass** (the natural home for badge sourcing, alongside the negative-badge sweep). Logged here rather than mass-editing piecemeal or fabricating citations. (Reversible; design law RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §4/§6/§9.)

The board FORECASTS the odds from the historical inputs the D74 model consumes; it never reads a rating at resolve-time. Triple-encoded + CVD-safe (number+grade+word+%); `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures.
- **DECIDED-&-LOGGED (scope):** Q7 = the GM layer's *read-out* (matchup + dual OVR) — fully buildable now on existing OOB+general data, byte-identical. ## D100 — RATING SYSTEM **Q8**: the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §15 / §14.6). A new "Camp" desk tab where, between battles, the President DRILLS the army; the drilled training raises the army he fields via a guarded, bounded conditioning seam — PURE INPUT-SEEDING, never the scoreboard, and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp**.
- **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; seeds `C.president.camp` = drill{musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**); `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged); `campSetDelegate`; `campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM — per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled); `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue, a delegated army auto-drills, a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's share ERODES — gated on `engaged`); `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`; `_campGrade`/`_campBar`. **Drilling/progression only** — SCOUTING deferred to Q8b (it needs the strategic-next-battle ↔ tactical-OOB mapping).
- **The bridge seam (`src/85-battle-bridge.js`):** `bridgeArmy` applies a guarded camp term — drilling lifts firepower (musketry) / morale (maneuver) / supply (entrenching) + relieves fatigue (endurance) + a small overall "sharpness," **bounded** (full-drill ≈ +8 overall over base, ≤14; fatigue DRAGS the gain ×(1−0.6·fat/100)). EXACTLY 0 when undrilled → byte-identical. Computed once, reused.
- **Wiring:** `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit); `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve); a "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js` (dispatch + tab arrays + button + wiring); `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` wholesale + lazy-migrates via idempotent campInit — **no `_SAVE_VER` bump** (additive, D7).
- **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop INERT until the player opens the camp — `campOnResolve` early-returns and `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill — so a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build (proven: probe-camp's keystone step + probe-bridge 6/6 + probe-conditioning 6/6 UNCHANGED). NO RNG (deterministic).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (21 Opus agents: 5 lenses × refute-verify + critic; 15 raw → 1 confirmed MED + 4 critic). ALL fixed: **(MED + a critic-MED, the real one)** the "bloody" attrition test divided a raw men-count by `C.manpower.strength` — a 0-100 INDEX (and one decremented upstream the same turn by manpowerOnResolve), so nearly every real battle read "bloody" → the **win-seasons branch was effectively DEAD** (drilled training only ever decayed, inverting the headline progression). FIXED: use the casualty **SHARE** (this side's casualties / both sides' total — unitless, order-independent; `ATTRITION_PIVOT` 0.18→0.55 share), and the probe SEASONING step re-tooled to REALISTIC casualties + a pyrrhic-win case (a won-but-bled-white battle correctly erodes). **(LOW)** `camp.lastTurn` dead code → removed; **(LOW)** a zero-guard comment overstated the invariant → corrected to foci-only; **(LOW)** drilling is a deliberate **player-only** lift (the AI does not drill; bounded by §27) → DECIDED-&-LOGGED here (any future enemy-preparedness model must be balanced against it). Re-vetted after the fixes.

## D101 — RATING SYSTEM **R-5**: the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person derivation + LAZY materialization + the play-as-anyone hook) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for: a brigade can now be *inspected down to its men*, and any person can be *materialized + promoted* — all PURE DATA + DISPLAY, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; the deterministic sim — sandbox + all 9 battles — is proven identical to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §5/§8/§9 R-5/§15 (R9).
- **The LAZY-MATERIALIZATION keystone (§8):** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` — its men's mean OVR, derived O(1) from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] (a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are NEVER instantiated en masse: `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand (inspect / play-as), and `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` builds a HARD-CAPPED (≤6) representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from a data-driven `musterTemplate`), **never `u.men` rows** — proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3. The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth.
- **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** `fldMenMeanOVR` · `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses the R-0 `fldDerivePerson` → headline + dual OVR + grade; a generated row gets a deterministic synthesized period name [`_fldSynthName` + `_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred provenance + a `latentCommand` seed) · `fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)` (the **latent-command promotion** = play-as-anyone: lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) · `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) · `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** §10 — Verified solid / Inferred HATCHED `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [✓/~/?] + word, NOT colour → CVD-safe) · `fldMusterHudLine` (the compact in-battle inspect line) · `fldMusterRollHtml` (the full "Muster Roll" panel, ready for the journey-mode character sheet). **Data:** `musterTemplate` + `_r5Note` added to `data/ratings.json`.
- **The ONLY live wiring:** one guarded line in `fldRenderHud` (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`) appends `fldMusterHudLine(u)` after the R-2 brigade-OVR line — so selecting a brigade now shows its **MEN OVR** (the men's prosopography mean) beside the R-2 combat OVR, with a provenance-hatched accent. Pure display; "" when ratings data absent → byte-identical. NO new combat path; NO RNG.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (11 agents: 4 diverse-lens Opus finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 6 raw → **2 confirmed + 2 critic, ALL LOW, ALL latent**; 0 HIGH/MED; completeness verdict: no no-fudge-wall write, no determinism leak, no lazy-materialization breach, no escaping gap). ALL 4 fixed (defensive-copy hardening so a FUTURE bulk-person/career path can't corrupt canonical `GAME_DATA`): **(1)** `fldMaterializePerson` returned the AUTHORED persona BY REFERENCE (via `fldDerivePerson`'s authored branch) → now shallow-copies persona at the materialization boundary; **(2)** `fldPromotePerson` with an unmapped/typo'd `toRank` silently mapped to the 64 anchor (a +16 unearned lift + false officerTier) → now requires a real `rankBase` key, else a clean no-op clone; **(3)** the `sources` ARRAY was a second shared reference (and `fldPromotePerson` propagated it) → now `.slice()`'d on both paths; **(4)** `fldPromotePerson`'s persona-less guard returned the input ref, breaking its "returns a NEW person" contract → added `_fldClonePerson` (copies persona + sources) for every no-op path. Re-vetted after the fixes.
- **Vetting:** GATE OK (no-fudge ✓); `probe-ratings` **19/19** (the R-5 step: one-mean-per-token bounded+deterministic+never-Legendary; the LAZY invariant [sample ≤6 for 100,000 men]; generated = Inferred + synth name + latentCommand; authored pass-through Verified; promotion surfaces command + is pure; team hook; Inferred-hatched vs Verified-solid distinct fills + distinct glyphs; render triple-encoded; purity; **+ the 4 bug-hunt hardening guards** — `aliasGuarded:true`); **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** vs committed HEAD `84c5e95` + R-5 live UI renders (0 pe); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe`/`t1probe` ok (the `load` suite worked this session, intermittent stalls cleared by retry); `probe-field` 13/13 + `probe-officers` 15/15 + `probe-command` 16/16 + `probe-desk` 13/13 + `probe-camp` 8/8 (0 pe each); `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures (lifted 5 sub-AA opacity values `.55/.6→.65` against the real dark-brown ground). **DECIDED-&-LOGGED:** the live wiring is the compact HUD line only (the full muster roll + promotion + team hooks ship as probe-vetted pure functions, ready for the post-R-5 GM depth-chart MOVES + the D93 journey mode — surfacing the roll in a dedicated inspect-expand / Army Register is a later UI pass). ## D102 — RATING SYSTEM **Q9**: the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE — promote · multi-currency · merit gate) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve, built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/political-capital spine + the R-5 person spine (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.2/§14.3/§15). The President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder, spending a **multi-currency** budget, **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display — **byte-identical until the player promotes** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Design law: §12.
- **The ladder + the move (`src/35-command.js`, the "Q9 (D102)" block):** `_cmdBaseGrade` parses each general's VERBOSE `generals.json` rank deterministically down to one of **Brig. Gen. → Maj. Gen. → Lt. Gen. → General** (the multi-word grades are checked before the bare "General"; an unrecognized rank defaults to the LOWEST grade — never invents a man up). `cmdPromote(C,id)` raises him one grade, spending BOTH currencies (gated on both): **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary — `capitalCost` by target grade, ×`aboveMeritMul` if above merit) + a NEW **seniority** pool (`cmd.seniority` — `seniorityCostBase` + a `seniorityLeapfrog` surcharge when he leapfrogs a passed-over senior). Bounded, clamped, logged.
- **The merit gate (the honest history):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep ≥ bar) → a confidence bump (+`earnedRepBonus`); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) → the capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation hit** (−`aboveMeritRepHit`). Because OVR = 0.55·skill + 0.45·reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** — rank without merit doesn't make a good commander. (Teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence.)
- **How it reaches the fight (no new combat path):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small BOUNDED amount — `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase delta × `skillLiftWeight` 0.92), clamped to `skillLiftCap` 6 — added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating → commandLeadership →` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). NEVER the scoreboard (D74/D94 no-fudge wall — `cmdPromote` mutates only `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation`). **0 lift when un-promoted → every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical.**
- **The surface + currency (`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdPromoRow`, new Command-desk section "The officer corps — promotions"):** each available general's current grade (↑ if promoted) + OVR + grade + a Promote control with the dual-currency cost + a merit annotation, above a capital + seniority read-out. Period-broadsheet styling; triple-encoded; CVD-safe (the grade dot is aria-hidden, meaning rides number+letter+word). `cmd.seniority` accrues over the campaign in `cmdOnResolve` (`seniorityPerTurn` + a `seniorityWinBonus`, capped) — a currency nothing combat reads, so the accrual is invisible/byte-identical. `data/ratings.json` gains the `promotion` config block. Rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump; idempotent `cmdInit` lazy-migration, D7).
- **DEFERRED-&-LOGGED (the rest of §12, mirrors Q7→R-5 / Q8→Q8b):** the **symmetric AI-GM** (the opponent drafts/promotes — needs enemy-commander→combat wiring; would break byte-identity / risk fudge), cross-theater **Transfer** (needs authored theaters — `generals.json` has none), **Commission** of generated officers + the full corps/division **depth-chart tree** (needs the strategic↔tactical OOB mapping — the Q8b blocker family). This slice ships the player-side promotion economy now; the loop proceeds once those substrates exist.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (7 Opus agents: 4 diverse-lens finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 2 raw → **2 confirmed + 1 actionable critic gap, ALL LOW, ALL latent**; 0 HIGH/MED; critic overall: *"SOUND and may be committed — the no-fudge wall, byte-identity, bounding, determinism, and no-exploit invariants all hold; no HIGH/MED missed."*). ALL 3 fixed: **(1)** `cmdPromote` gated on `Math.round(capital)` but spent from raw `capital` → a fractional balance could pass the rounded gate and be floor-absorbed on the spend → now debits the same rounded `cap` (byte-identical under every current integer-only capital path). **(2)** `_cmdBaseGrade`'s unrecognized-rank fallback was "Maj. Gen." (rankBase 68) → would over-grade a future non-named officer (e.g. a Colonel, 64) two grades onto the General ladder → now defaults to the LOWEST grade "Brig. Gen." (unreachable on the shipped surface; hardens the deferred depth-chart path). **(3, critic)** `cmdInit` re-seeded `seniority` only when invalid → a valid-but-out-of-band tampered/stale save value wasn't re-clamped until the next resolve → now clamps to the cap on LOAD. The critic's other gap (the two `diag-classic` 404s) is the **pre-existing documented tolerated asset-layer 404 noise**, not Q9 (Q9 touches no asset paths). Re-vetted after the fixes.
- **Vetting:** GATE OK (no-fudge ✓); `probe-command` **25/25** (16 prior + **9 new Q9 steps**: seniority seeded + empty promotions [byte-identical default]; the save-tamper LOAD re-clamp; the grade-ladder parse [Lee=General / Grant=Lt. Gen. / Meade & Stuart=Maj. Gen.]; Lee [top grade] not promotable; promotion GATED when either currency is short + SPENDS both + stores the grade; EARNED raises rep / ABOVE-MERIT costs more capital + cuts rep; a promotion lifts effective skill [bounded ≤6] → reaches commandLeadership, un-promoted byte-identical; every general both sides reads the SAME skill with/without C; the render surfaces the section + currencies + a Promote control), 0 pe; **byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** vs committed HEAD `fc1d251` + the Q9 live sanity (a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79→80 [bounded], renders the section, un-promoted reads identical, 0 pe); `probe-ratings` 19/19 + `probe-desk` 13/13 + `probe-camp` 8/8 + `t1probe` 14/14 (0 pe each); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` ok; `wcag-auditor` 0 AA failures (fixed the new warning text `#c2502e`→`#d66040`, 4.51:1 measured against the real dark `.sheet` ground). **ENV:** the `load` suite stalled intermittently on the THREE-CDN headless load this session (the documented gotcha — cleared by a fresh threaded server + retry); the `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness remains the authoritative no-regression proof. ## D103 — RATING SYSTEM **R-6 (citation-provenance portion)**: the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The R-6 increment's **negative-badge ASSIGNMENT to rosters + live dev-traits remain**; this milestone shipped the **citation-grade prerequisite** that gates them: every `Verified`-stamped claim in the data catalog now carries **≥2 independent real sources**, the non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build. **A live violation was found and closed:** an audit revealed the debt was NOT confined to badges (the logged D98–D101 framing) — **47 records across SIX data files** were stamped `Verified` with <2 sources (badges 13 · personas 2 · weapons 9 · artillery 9 · engineering 8 · terrain 1 · cabinet 5). PURE METADATA + a little teaching-card text — **byte-identical sim** (all 10 deterministic battles IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `5b12916`; no numeric combat field touched, bug-hunt-confirmed).
- **The citation workflow (the ultracode pattern):** a 15-agent research+verify Workflow (7 domains: per-domain Opus finders → **default-refute** adversarial verifiers → a completeness critic; sources **web-checked**; discipline = NEVER fabricate, **downgrade-to-Inferred over guess**). Outcome: **0 fabrication** (critic-confirmed), all citations real/on-claim/independent. Two judgment calls logged: **`beloved` held *Inferred*** (its one solid cite is Symonds 1997 on Cleburne; the obvious Lee source — Freeman 1934 — is Lost-Cause-tinged and held out until a non-hagiographic Lee cite is added), and **`grand_charge` upgraded *Verified*** (Stewart 1959 · Hess 2001 · Sears 2003, satisfying its in-data "Inferred until the sweep" note). Anti-Lost-Cause cut both ways: `feared`'s second cite was swapped Wyeth 1899 (Lost-Cause-era hagiography) → **Hurst 1993** (modern critical bio); the NEGATIVE badges on real men carry the firmest pairs (Sears+Rafuse, Marvel+O'Reilly, Cozzens+Daniel, McMurry+Sword).
- **The permanent gate (`tools/build.mjs` 4e, the keystone):** a recursive scan of every `data/*.json` — any record whose `prov`/`provenance` is "Verified" (matched **trim+case-normalized on EITHER key**, so a whitespace/case variant or an `Inferred`-masks-`Verified` pairing cannot erode it) with a `sources`/`src` array of <2 → `die(5)`. **Verified firing on all 47 before the fix; passes after** (`GATE OK · … · citations ✓`). The long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (…)", "Verified (high) — …", ~72 of them) cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to ≠ "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. Mirrors the 4d no-fudge wall: a non-negotiable made structural.
- **Accuracy fixes folded in (critic-surfaced, false-claims-under-Verified):** the Fredericksburg `cover-killing-ground` card's "almost impregnable, and a deathtrap" was **misattributed to the NPS** (the phrase traces to a fan site) → paraphrased, no false attribution; `massed_battery`'s note dropped "Pelham" (Fredericksburg, not covered by its Gettysburg sources); `earned_in_blood` tightened to "14 of the 16 Medals of Honor awarded to Black soldiers (Army)"; the Springfield "~1.5M" and three art-cs-handicap dates softened to match the sourced precision; the Whitworth flavor reconciled.

Player-visible upside: the engineering/cabinet/teaching cards that render their provenance now display the real citations.

## D105 — RATING SYSTEM **LIVE DEV-TRAITS (the Madden development arc)**: a general's OVR now develops over the campaign, shaped by a hidden potential ceiling — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The last open item on the R-6 rating track (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §9-R-6: "reputation level-up → OVR still TODO") + the D94-fork-#5 lock ("Reputation→OVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign now"). `cmdOnResolve` already evolved a general's reputation by battle outcome (decisive win +6 / win +3 / draw −1 / loss −4 / decisive loss −8), and `_cmdGenRating` (0.55·skill + 0.45·reputation) → `commandLeadership` already read it — so winning a campaign already nudged his OVR. D105 adds the **Madden DEV-TRAIT** that SHAPES that arc: a hidden potential **ceiling** (how high he can climb), a **floor** (how far he can fall), a development **rate** (rise vs fall), and an **attritionDrag** (the §15-R3 decline-with-heavy-attrition). **ACCURATE INPUTS, never an output gate (D74/D92)** — a dev-trait only shapes the general's REPUTATION (an INPUT the existing pipe consumes), it NEVER writes a casualty/winner. Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §9-R-6 / §14.6 / §15-R3.
- **The keystone (byte-identical-when-off, the R-6/D104 pattern):** the engine seam in `cmdOnResolve` is **byte-identical for an UNASSIGNED general (or absent devTraits data)** — it takes the LITERAL pre-D105 path `clamp(cur+delta, 5, 98)`, rate 1, no drag (proven across ALL five outcome quadrants + both clamp rails). The deliberate, citation-grade, historically-directed change is the AUTHORED `data/ratings.json` `devTraits.assign` map (20 generals → one of 12 archetypes). The ceiling/floor are RELATIVE to the general's SEEDED start reputation (`devTrack.start`, fixed), every archetype keeps `ceilingAbove≥5 & floorBelow≥5`, so the pre-D105 "a winning general gains reputation / a losing one loses it" invariant holds for all.
- **The arc (in `cmdOnResolve`):** an assigned general's base delta is scaled by his `riseRate`/`fallRate`, plus a bounded extra `attritionDrag` when his side bled the lion's share (casualty SHARE > pivot — the D100 unit-correct measure), then clamped to HIS `[floor,ceiling]` band. New pure fns (`src/35-command.js`): `_cmdDevCfg`/`_cmdDevStart`/`_cmdDevTrait` (resolves the absolute band) / `_cmdAttritionDrag` (bounded ≤ attritionDragMax) / `_cmdDevTrackUpdate` (pure observation) / `_cmdDevTrend` / `_cmdCareerArcHTML`. `cmdInit` seeds + sanitizes `cmd.devTrack[id]={start,peak,low,battles}` (rides the save, no `_SAVE_VER` bump). NO RNG.
- **The 12 archetypes + anti-Lost-Cause balance:** rising_star (Grant/Sherman/Sheridan) · steady_rock (Thomas) · established_legend (Lee/Jackson) · natural_genius (Forrest) · steady_professional (Meade/Scott→administrator/Longstreet/A.S.Johnston) · cautious_fabian (J.E.Johnston) · mercurial_cavalier (Stuart/Beauregard) · administrator (Scott/Halleck) · plateau (McClellan) · overpromoted (Burnside/Hooker) · volatile_aggressor (Hood) · quarrelsome (Bragg). **The thesis is anti-Lost-Cause:** the Union's elite are RISERS (4 high-ceiling developers rated as high as Lee/Jackson — the honest claim that the Union found and elevated its best command) while command failures are named plainly on BOTH sides (US McClellan plateau / Burnside-Hooker overpromoted; CS Bragg quarrelsome / Hood volatile-disaster). All 20 assignments are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading of a documented arc — gate-4e-exempt) with 1-2 real sources each; nothing laundered (Forrest's Klan + Longstreet's Lost-Cause slander named in the notes).
- **The read-out (`_cmdCareerArcHTML`, a new Command-desk "Career Arc" section):** the sitting general's dev-trait tier (label + glyph + polarity sign + desc), his OVR arc (start→now→peak on a floor..ceiling band with start/peak ticks), a trend verdict (Rising/Holding/Fading/Untested) + the net delta, and a soft potential-room note. Triple-encoded (word + sign + number; glyph + colour decorative) → CVD-safe; `wcag-auditor` AA (one nested-opacity spot 3.93→4.57:1 fixed).
- **The no-fudge wall extended (bug-hunt):** build-gate 4d (the no-fudge OUTPUT WALL) now also scans `src/35-command.js` (confirmed it writes ONLY command state — reputation/seniority/capital/devTrack, none in the forbidden set) — closing the coverage gap so the strategic rating code's no-fudge invariant is STRUCTURAL too (mirrors how D103's gate 4e made citations un-erodable).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (the ultracode pattern — 5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge · byte-identity · bounding/determinism · citation/balance · UI/probe] × default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 29 agents; **8 confirmed + 3 critic-missed; 1 HIGH, 3 MED, 7 LOW; critic: "SAFE TO COMMIT — both hard invariants [no output gate, byte-identical-when-off] CONFIRMED HOLD"** via independent grep corroboration that `devTrack`/`reputation` are read by no combat code). ALL 11 fixed: **(HIGH, the only blocker)** a fabricated-by-misattribution Thomas citation ("Conquered into Liberty" is Eliot Cohen's, not Larry Daniel's) → corrected to Daniel's actual *Days of Glory: The Army of the Cumberland* (CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #4); **(MED)** the Burnside note "proved right at Fredericksburg" laundered a Union command failure → rewritten to name the futile Marye's-Heights assaults plainly (anti-Lost-Cause); **(MED, the keystone hardening)** `_cmdDevTrait`/`_cmdDevStart` consumed `devTrack.start` RAW → a tampered/stale save (start NaN / 500) poisoned the reputation clamp → now coerced through `_cmdNum` + clamped [0,100] at the read site, `cmdInit` SANITIZES the whole record on LOAD (the Q9 re-clamp pattern), and `_cmdCareerArcHTML` coerces the whole `tr` record (no "NaN" can render); **(MED→the gate gap above);** **(LOW ×7)** byte-identical-off probe now covers all 5 quadrants + both clamp rails; the off-test asserts `devTraits.assign` is restored (no global-state leak); floor/drag steps assert the locked general's trait; the render step covers all 4 `_cmdDevTrend` branches + the battles=0 edge; the new SAVE-TAMPER probe step (start NaN/500/−99 → finite + in-band + no NaN render); the balance check counts named-failures as (−,~) so it doesn't rest on the single cs-bragg record.
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK · no-fudge ✓` (4d now scans 35-command.js) `· citations ✓` (the Thomas fix); `probe-command` **34/34** (9 D105 steps: data+balance · byte-identical-off all-quadrants+rails · assign-restored · rising-star-vs-plateau+ceiling · floor cap · attrition drag bounded · no-output-gate+devTrack-purity · save-tamper · render+4 trend branches); `probe-ratings` **21/21** (the tactical rating engine + the 9-battle badge resolution intact — D105 touches NO tactical code, byte-identical by construction, confirmed by `git diff`), `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA. **ENV:** the 8 GB Mac had a healthy memory window this session; probes ran foreground via a threaded server (the documented load-stall gotcha did not bite). Committed + pushed only after the full empirical gate passed. (Reversible; non-negotiables honored: D74/D92 no-output-gate + the empirical-vet-before-push gate.)

## D133 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · H1 increment 1: **THE OFFLINE PORTRAIT TIER + THE D71 ASSET-INGESTION PIPELINE** — the single-file deliverable's public-domain portraits now show even when it is opened standalone (no `assets/` folder beside it), via a small compressed tier the build inlines into `__ASSETS` — [AARON go/no-go + CLAUDE impl] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
**THE GATED FORK — surfaced + cleared (AskUserQuestion):** H1/H2 (PD imagery + reenactment footage) is the ONE external-asset / network-fetch / IP-licensing / single-file-stressing roadmap item, flagged by every doc as NOT unattended-safe. Aaron chose **"Go on H1/H2 now"** (present to review assets). Increment 1 builds the **D71 ingestion pipeline + embeds the ALREADY-PD-vetted, in-repo portraits** (no NEW external fetch this increment — the 155 `assets/portraits/*.jpg` were downloaded + Commons-PD-gated in run-h) as the pipeline's proving ground; subsequent increments (weapons / flags / scenes / USCT / footage) fetch NEW assets, each surfaced for per-asset licence + anachronism sign-off.
- **THE GAP IT CLOSES (recon).** The frozen base.html PD-photo layer (`_warmPhotos`) loads `assets/portraits/<key>.jpg` by RELATIVE PATH → the real photos show only when the file is served beside `assets/`; opened standalone they 404 to the procedural engraving. So the deliverable was not truly portable for photos. (The in-game "131 portraits" were the PROCEDURAL engravings; 155 real PD photos sat on disk, unembedded.)
- **WHAT SHIPPED (3 files + the tier).** (1) `tools/prep-embed-assets.mjs` (NEW) — the TIER/COMPRESS half of D71: macOS `sips` shrinks `assets/portraits/*.jpg` → `assets/embed/portraits/` (≤128px, q64; 155 files, 953KB; committed as deliverable source). (2) `tools/build.mjs` (EDIT) — a new stage Base64-inlines `assets/embed/**` into a bare-name global `var __ASSETS = {"portraits/<stem>":"data:image/jpeg;base64,…"}` with a HARD (3.0MB) / SOFT (1.5MB) byte budget, a duplicate-key gate, a `withFileTypes` non-file skip, and a report line; plus a `"data:…"` string-literal MASK before the HEX_BOMB textual scan (a megabyte of base64 textually trips the naive `0x…[g-z]` pattern, while `node --check` already proves real parseability). (3) `src/21-photo-embed.js` (NEW module, manifest after `20-president-render.js`) — overrides `window.portraitFor`: base hi-res relative-path photo (data:image/jpeg) wins when present, else this embedded 128px tier (offline-safe, framed by a pixel-faithful copy of base `_framePhoto`/`_photoMount`), else the base engraving (data:image/png); + a `.lead-badge` MutationObserver upgrade (the base observer calls the CLOSURE `portraitFor`, not `window`). The build grew 3.1MB → 4.3MB (well within D34.4 "several MB; don't trade scope for bytes").
- **ARCHITECTURE — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat / data / save file; the module reads ONLY the new `__ASSETS` global + (read-only) the lead-badge DOM, writes NO sim field, NEVER `fldRng`, no save-version bump. It only swaps an `<img>` source on presentation surfaces. NO-OP when `__ASSETS` carries no portraits (then byte-identical to pre-H1). Proven by `probe-presets` **26/26** seed-for-seed + `probe-phased-ab` **20/20 (0 diffs)**.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (6 diverse-lens Opus finders → 8 raw findings; D74-purity lens returned 0 → byte-identity clean; ALL real findings FIXED + re-vetted; the workflow's verify/critic legs dragged on the 8 GB Mac so they were substituted by inline code-verification + a standalone completeness-critic agent on the FIXED code, the D124/D128/D132 precedent).** **(MED — the standout, confirmed by code-trace)** `_pheUpgrade` DOWNGRADED a base hi-res lead-badge photo to the 128px embedded tier when served-from-root: a badge created AFTER base hi-res warms gets hi-res from the base CLOSURE `portraitFor` but carries no `data-portrait-photo` flag, so an attribute guard missed it → **FIXED** to skip any `<img>` already showing a `data:image/jpeg` (a src sniff, never a downgrade) + a new `probe-photo-embed` NO-DOWNGRADE assertion locks it. **(MED/LOW — perf)** the original eager-warm framed all 155 portraits at boot, pure waste served-from-root (base hi-res covers them) → **FIXED** to LAZY per-key framing, with the full tier eager-warmed ONLY when a one-shot probe image (`assets/portraits/<stem>.jpg?phe=1`) 404s (offline) → served-from-root frames ~nothing. **(LOW ×3 — build)** a stray sub-dir named like an asset crashed the build with EISDIR → **FIXED** `withFileTypes` skip; two sources differing only by extension silently collided to one `__ASSETS` key → **FIXED** a duplicate-key die; no per-file size cap → **FIXED** a prep per-file warn. **(MED — honesty)** "offline-portable" is true FOR PORTRAITS ONLY (the 3D terrain/HDRI/GLB still resolve by relative path) → documented as the scope, the future H1 categories. The standalone critic verdict on the fixed code: **SAFE TO COMMIT.**

## D132 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · BASE-ENGINE FIX: **MULTI-PHASE 3D SCENE REBUILD** — the live 3D scene now rebuilds when a multi-phase battle advances a phase (the new unit cast becomes visible, the prior phase's meshes are disposed, the woods/walls/objective-beacon move to the new sector, the camera re-frames it) — fixing a PRE-EXISTING base bug D131's bug-hunt surfaced — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The combat-path candidate Aaron chose (AskUserQuestion) over the H1/H2 external-asset layer (deferred — needs Aaron present for the per-asset IP/licensing review). **The bug (pre-existing, git-traced to predate T10/H1b — D131's bug-hunt SURFACED it, not introduced it):** the 4 multi-phase battles (Antietam · Gettysburg · Chickamauga · Vicksburg — 4 of the 9 shipped) each run as sequential phases, and recon confirmed **every phase declares its own distinct sector terrain (own woods/walls) AND its own objective**. On a 3D phase advance the engine (`_fldAdvancePhase`→`_fldBuildPhase`, T8) swapped in a FRESH unit cast (new ids), fresh terrain, and a fresh objective, but **never rebuilt the live 3D scene** → the new brigades got no `_u3d` group (INVISIBLE), the prior phase's groups + officer/supply/arms/eng meshes ORPHANED, and the woods/walls/objective-beacon stayed at the OLD sector. (2D was unaffected — it reads live state each frame; the headless sim was unaffected — no 3D. So the bug only ever showed in real 3D play of a multi-phase battle.)
- **EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED FIRST (the prompt's requirement):** a NEW `tools/probe-phased-3d.mjs` drove each of the 4 battles in the live 3D renderer + advanced every phase exactly as the engine does, asserting the CORRECT post-fix invariants. Run against the **pre-fix** build it FAILED decisively (Antietam phase-1 `coverage=0` [4 units, 0 groups], `orphans=6`, the beacon stranded `dz=65` off the new objective at phase 2; Gettysburg the same) — confirming both symptoms (invisible new units AND stale terrain/objective) before a line was changed.
- **THE FIX (presentation-only; combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION — D74):** new `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene()` (T0), called from `_fldAdvancePhase` (T8) ONLY when `__FIELD.mode3d`, re-runs the same per-phase build sequence as `fld3dInit` — `fld3dBuildTerrain()` (fresh ground/objective-ring+beacon/walls/markers/woods/water) + `fld3dBuildUnits()` (the fresh cast; the T10 wrapper re-skins flags) + officers/supply/arms/flags/eng — then `_fld3dReaimPhase()` reseats the survey camera onto the new objective (B-6 side-aware). The scene-level per-phase terrain meshes are now tracked via `_fld3dTrackPhase` into `__FIELD._phaseScene[]` and disposed by `_fld3dDisposePhaseScene()` at the TOP of `fld3dBuildTerrain` (the renderer/camera/lights/scene/groups container persist; every unit-scoped builder already self-disposes). **The headless stepper (renderer 'none' → `mode3d` false) NEVER enters the rebuild → the sim is untouched.**
- **BYTE-IDENTITY PROVEN THREE WAYS:** `probe-presets` **26/26** (the difficulty/byte-identity gate); a NEW `tools/probe-phased-ab.mjs` headless A/B sweep (4 battles × 5 seeds × the committed pre-fix build vs the fixed build) = **20 comparisons, 0 diffs** — winner/winBy/per-side casualties/phase-score/per-phase-log/steps identical number-for-number (and historically faithful: Antietam CS-tactical, Gettysburg/Vicksburg US, Chickamauga CS); and all 4 per-battle outcome probes green (their committed expected outcomes are the pre-fix baselines). No combat/data/save file touched; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; never `fldRng`.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (6 diverse-lens Opus finders → the 4 findings, ALL FIXED).** The finders returned **4 findings, all one class — a GPU-buffer leak the rebuild introduced by re-calling builders that weren't self-disposing:** **(HIGH + MED, same bug)** `fld3dBuildEng` (T13) did a bare `parent.remove(_engGroup)` (detach WITHOUT traverse-disposing) then dropped the mesh refs → a phase with entrenchments/abatis/pontoons (the Vicksburg siege) orphaned their geometries/materials on every advance, and the detached group escaped `fld3dDispose`'s scene-traverse at exit too → **FIXED** self-disposing (`_fld3dDisposeGroup(_engGroup)` first — the berm/abatis/pontoon meshes are its children — matching every other builder; does NOT touch water); **(MED)** `fld3dBuildWater` (T13) disposed its prior `_waterGroup` only AFTER the no-river early-return → a river→no-river phase advance left a stale + leaked river → **FIXED** by moving the dispose ABOVE the early-return; **(LOW)** the T8 rebuild call site fully swallowed exceptions, masking the very invisible-brigade failure D132 fixes → **FIXED** to `console.warn` (a real failure now surfaces + a probe's console gate catches it; the phase still advances). A **completeness self-check** then confirmed EVERY builder `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene` calls now self-disposes (terrain via `_phaseScene`, markers/beacon tracked, units/officers/supply/arms self-dispose, flags idempotent, eng + water now self-dispose) → the leak surface is fully closed. (The hunt's automated verify+critic legs were env-blocked — a hung 6th finder + an OOM on the 8 GB Mac during the focused re-run — so they were substituted by inline code-verification of all 4 findings + a standalone completeness-critic agent + the empirical re-vet, the D124/D128 substitution precedent.)
- **Re-vet after the fixes (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-phased-3d` **64/64** (all 4 battles, every phase: coverage=1 · 0 orphans · groupsChildren==units · the beacon re-seats on the new objective at every phase · woods rebuilt per sector · non-blank render · 0 pageerrors · 0 texture warnings) — re-confirmed AFTER the T13 fixes; `probe-presets` **26/26** re-confirmed post-fix; `probe-phased-ab` **20/20 0 diffs**; `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 · `probe-weather` 30/30 · `probe-render-richness` 30/30 · `probe-audio-ambience` 22/22 · `probe-flags` 36/36 · `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (the atmospheric/flag stack coexists); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; VISUALLY CONFIRMED (the captured Burnside's-Bridge phase-2 shot now shows the fresh sector + visible brigades + the re-seated beacon under T17's dawn fog — previously empty). `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction (no new DOM/UI — only a camera re-aim + 3D mesh rebuild). **ENV:** `probe-engineering`/`probe-engineering-corps` are `waitUntil:'load'` → blocked by the documented THREE-CDN headless load-stall (D97/D110), NOT a regression — the eng/water 3D builders are instead exercised by the `domcontentloaded` `probe-phased-3d` (which drives them through 12 phase advances) + `probe-tactical-visuals`. **Committed + pushed only after the full empirical gate passed.** (Reversible; non-negotiables honored: D74 combat byte-identity proven 3 ways · the empirical-vet-before-push gate · base.html untouched.)

## D131 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · H1b: **FLAGS & INSIGNIA DEEPENING** — citation-grade battle-aware flag selection + corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES (date-gated to the 1863 fields) drawn on the 2D/3D unit markers + the selected-brigade HUD, DEEPENING the existing `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The H1b increment per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 5 + memory `civilwar-idea-brigade-battle-flags`. **`T10-flags.js` ALREADY existed** (a basic flag/insignia layer shipped earlier) → H1b DEEPENS it (the D91 deepen-not-replace ethic); it does NOT add a new module. Recon of the prior code found **three real defects, all fixed here:** (1) the 2D path computed an SVG + a `new Image()` it NEVER drew → 2D flags rendered as blank solid-colour rectangles; (2) corps-badge SHAPES were never drawn (only a text label), and the shape MAP was wrong — II Corps was a circle (should be a TREFOIL), V and VI were both a generic "cross"; (3) corps badges showed on ALL battles regardless of date (an anachronism on the 1861-62 fields), and a roman-numeral substring match mis-read "II Corps" as "I Corps".
- **What shipped (the deepening):** (1) **battle-AWARE flag selection** — a new `_FLD_BATTLE_META` table (date/theater/badge-eligibility per scenario) drives the Confederate "default" flag: **First National "Stars and Bars"** at First Bull Run (the ANV battle flag did NOT exist on 21 Jul 1861 — its very creation was prompted by the smoke-confusion of the Stars and Bars with the U.S. flag THAT day) and in the early West (Shiloh), the **ANV battle flag (Southern Cross)** for the mid-war East, the **Hardee pattern** (blue field + white disc) for the native Army of Tennessee, with **Longstreet's transferred Eastern brigades (Hood/Kershaw/Law) flying the ANV flag even at Chickamauga**; (2) **NEW flag patterns drawn for real** (the doc once claimed an unimplemented "hardee") — first-national, hardee, polk (upright St-George cross, distinct from the ANV diagonal saltire), and a US cavalry guidon, all procedural canvas; (3) **corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES drawn as glyphs** — I=disc, II=trefoil, III=diamond, V=Maltese (a flared cross pattée), VI=Greek cross (plain, distinct from V), XI=crescent, XII=star — coloured by division (1st=red/2nd=white/3rd=blue) and ALWAYS paired with a text label (CVD-safe: shape + label, never colour alone), with a light parchment **halo** so the shape silhouette reads on any background; (4) the **anachronism GATE** — badges (adopted by Hooker's Circular of 21 Mar 1863) appear ONLY at the Eastern post-Mar-1863 fields (here Chancellorsville + Gettysburg) and NEVER on Bull Run / Malvern Hill / Antietam / Fredericksburg (where the corps existed but wore no badge yet — the HUD names the adoption date there as a teaching beat); (5) a **working 2D draw** (a cached canvas blit, fog-gated) + a deepened **HUD** (the flag thumbnail + the badge swatch + a citation-grade provenance caption).
- **CITATION-GRADE CONTENT (a research+verify Workflow, 25 agents: 6 Opus historian-finders × 3-lens default-refute verifiers + a synthesis):** the verified fact-sheet CONFIRMED the core code and surfaced two refinements I applied — the **Chickamauga ANV-transplant split** (Hood/Kershaw were Longstreet's Eastern divisions, ANV flag) and **Vicksburg** flying a Western pattern (Pemberton's Western-lineage army), not the Eastern ANV cross — plus a doc-citation softening ("General Orders No. 53" → "Hooker's Circular of 21 March 1863"; the surviving primary artifact is a Headquarters AotP circular, the No. 53 label under-attested; the DATE is solid). ≥2 independent reputable sources per flag/badge/date (Encyclopedia Virginia · Smithsonian NMAH · Britannica · confederateflags.org · Tennessee State Museum · crwflags.com FOTW · Washington Times · Gettysburg Flag Works · American Battlefield Trust), anti-Lost-Cause (the battle flag's origin framed factually as a post-Manassas battlefield-recognition device, not romanticized).
- **ARCHITECTURE — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. The render fns (`fldDrawFlags` 2D / `fld3dBuildFlags` 3D / `fldFlagHudSelected` HUD) are reached only through the EXISTING T0 `typeof` seams (probes drive the sim headlessly and never call them). Reads sim state READ-ONLY (`u.name/side/x/z/facing/alive/state`, `__FIELD.scenario/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng`, bumps no save-version. The install block wraps ONLY `fld3dBuildUnits`/`fld3dDispose` (disposal of flag+corps-badge CanvasTextures, + a reinforcement re-skin) via a generic `_fldFlagKeep` that propagates any prior introspection markers (the D130 lesson) — these are NOT the T16/T17/T18/T19 marker-bearing fns, so no chain is shadowed (probe-confirmed the `._atmo`/`._wx` chain stays intact). Diff = `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` (deepened) + `tools/probe-flags.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat / data / save file touched** → all 9 battles byte-identical seed-for-seed (probe-presets 26/26).
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity · fog-leak · history/Lost-Cause · robustness · perf/GPU · a11y/DOM] × 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 46 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 CONFIRMED finding (3/3) + 6 critic areas → 3 in-scope fixes applied, 1 base bug SURFACED, 2 noted:** **(CONFIRMED, MED — a PRE-EXISTING base T0/T8 bug, git-traced to predate T10 → SURFACED, NOT fixed in this presentation-only milestone):** a phased-battle 3D phase-advance (`_fldBuildPhase`/`_fldAdvancePhase` in the combat-path T8) swaps in new unit ids but never rebuilds the `_u3d` 3D groups → new-phase units get no 3D group + the prior phase's groups orphan; H1b only marginally enlarges the orphaned-mesh footprint by adding CanvasTextures.
