## D130 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · H4: **BATTLE-AMBIENCE AUDIO DEEPENING** — a default-OFF, opt-in, stereo-spatialized procedural battle-soundscape bed (rolling-fire wash + gated cannonade sub-bass + fog-gated located cannon/musket reports) UNDER the existing T9 din+SFX — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The H4 increment per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 4 + the D91 "continue audio incrementally" decision. The base.html `dinSet` din already gives a MONO intensity bed (rumble + cannon thump + musket crackle), and T9-audio.js (D77) bridges it into the modern tactical engine. H4 DEEPENS the subsystem with a NEW layer — it does NOT replace T9. **Sub-choice decided-&-logged:** a NEW `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` module (the T16/T17/T18 wrap-by-assignment precedent) rather than editing T9 in place — lowest-risk, idiomatic, keeps the SFX bridge intact. PROCEDURAL WebAudio synthesis only ($0 / single-file — no external sound files; the linked-asset audio fork remains un-started + would be SURFACED first).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` — a spatialized "great-battle" bed layered UNDER T9's din+SFX, pairing 1:1 with the T16 gunsmoke (sound comes from where the smoke rises): (1) a continuous **rolling-fire wash** (looping band-passed noise + a slow swell-LFO tremolo, gain tracking battle intensity — the "one continuous roar"); (2) a **cannonade sub-bass rumble** (looping low-passed brown noise, gated up by the count of brigades actually working their guns); (3) **located cannon/musket reports** — a cannon = sharp crack + body thump + rolling reverberant tail; a musket = a filtered-noise volley "rip" — each panned in stereo by the firing brigade's field-x (side-corrected to the camera end) and **fog-gated** (a hidden foe makes no located sound). Discoverable via a new accessible "Battle ambience" On/Off row appended to T9's audio panel; one-time captioned through T9's accessible caption.
- **ARCHITECTURE — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dRender` / `fld2dDraw` (drive the per-frame decision tick, throttled) / `fldExit` (dispose) / T9's `_fldAudioPanelRows` (append the toggle row) BY ASSIGNMENT — with a generic `keep()` helper that propagates EVERY prior introspection marker (`._atmo`/`._wx`/`._t9audio`/T18's) onto each new wrapper so the sibling probes still see the chain (a regression the no-regression sweep caught mid-build — fixed before commit). OWNS a separate AudioContext (the AUDIO_SCORE / SOUND one-context-per-subsystem convention). Reads ONLY render + read-only sim fields (`u._artFlash`/`u.targetId`/`u.ammo`/`u.state`/`u.x`/`u.id`/`u.side`/`u.alive`, `__FIELD.phase/paused/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng` (no randomness reaches the sim — audio texture uses `Math.random` like base.html's din), no `_SAVE_VER` (the `battleAmbience` flag is lazy-defaulted). The SCHEDULING DECISIONS (intensity, fog-gate, pan) are recorded in a `FLDAMB` state object whether or not a real audio device exists → fully testable headless. Diff = `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T19 after T18) + `tools/probe-audio-ambience.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. Proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a per-pure-render-window sim-seed-invariance assertion (240× `fldAmbUpdate`, seed unmoved).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** **DEFAULT-OFF** (`G.settings.battleAmbience !== true` → zero sound, never built — the byte-identical-mix default), **fully suppressed under `reduceMotion`** (the calm default — the T16 convention), volume scaled by the existing `battleLoud` (off→silent) AND the master capped low (≤0.20, under the din's 0.26) so it never overwhelms the cues it sits under ("never jarring"). Located reports defer until the AudioContext is genuinely running (no first-gesture stampede); the bed self-silences on the 'over' screen (no idle-graph drain); source-voices node-pool bounded + all nodes disposed + context suspended on `fldExit`. CVD-safe (no colour-encoded info); the toggle row reuses T9's AA-vetted segmented-button markup (keyboard / focus / aria-pressed) → `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity · webaudio-leaks · fog-leak · edge-robust · a11y-ux · lifecycle] × 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 19 agents; critic confidence HIGH; "NO byte-identity violation, NO fog leak, marker-chain correct").** **1 confirmed + 2 critic-surfaced real edge-bugs + 1 LOW refinement, ALL FIXED:** **(CONFIRMED, MED, 3/3)** `fldAmbCaptionOnce` burned the one-shot `captioned` flag BEFORE the caption rendered — but T9's `_fldAudioCaption` no-ops when captions are off (the default), so a user enabling captions mid-battle would never see the cue the layer advertises → the flag is now consumed ONLY inside the captions-on branch (re-checked cheaply each tick until shown). **(CRITIC, MED)** the six lenses only saw the probe's always-running context; in the real game the context is born SUSPENDED until a gesture, and located reports kept scheduling against the frozen clock → a stacked "stampede" the instant audio resumed → `fldAmbReports` now gates on `ctx.state === "running"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** the live WebAudio graph idled indefinitely on the post-battle 'over' screen (master never zeroed there) → `fldAmbUpdate` now silences on `phase === "over"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** StereoPanner nodes shared the source bag, diluting the documented voice cap + a dead `.stop()` per dispose → panners moved to a separate `pans` pool (cap counts audible voices only; panners disconnect-only). Probe strengthened 19→22 steps (the suspended-ctx gate, the 'over'-silence, the panner-pool disposal).

## D129 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · H3-i3: **TERRAIN & UNIT RENDER RICHNESS** — procedural ground texture + woods wind-sway + banner cloth ripple + selection/march polish + casualty fade — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The next Phase-H increment after H3-i2 (D128), per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 3. A NEW presentation-only module makes the battlefield itself feel alive — the ground grows real texture, the woods sway, the colours ripple, marching columns bob, and a fallen brigade fades from the field instead of snapping out. Continues leading H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` — (1) **3D ground vertex-colour enrichment** (procedural grass mottle + dry-ochre / damp-lush / bare-earth patches + tilled crop-row corduroy in a "cultivated" mask — positions untouched, colours only); (2) **woods wind-sway** (per-cone tilt-about-base on the InstancedMesh); (3) **banner cloth ripple** (per-unit flag twist/dip, ties H1b flags); (4) **selection-ring pulse** + a **march bob** for moving brigades; (5) a **casualty fade-out** on death (the group settles into the ground + fades over ~0.85s). Plus 2D-canvas equivalents (a cached soft field-grain, a pulsing selection halo, the same casualty fade).
- **ARCHITECTURE — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dBuildTerrain` (enrich + capture) / `fld3dRender` (frame hook) / `fld3dSyncUnit` (per-unit polish) / `fld2dDraw` (2D) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16/T17 seam; propagates the `._wx`/`._atmo` markers so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). All variation is **analytic value-noise + wall-clock sines — NEVER `fldRng`**; reads ONLY render state + read-only sim fields (`u.x`/`u.z`/`u.alive`/`u.state`/`u.id`, `__FIELD.sel`); writes NO sim field, no `_SAVE_VER`. The ground enrichment recolors VERTICES only — units seat on the analytic `fldTerrainH`, not the mesh, so they never float/sink. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT:** `renderRich="off"` (or a fresh launch with it set) leaves the un-enriched ground + unswayed woods + flat flags. Diff = `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T18 after T17) + `tools/probe-render-richness.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat/data/save file touched** — proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a new per-burst sim-field-invariance probe assertion (x/z/men/morale/facing/formation unchanged across 200 render frames).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** every MOTION effect (woods sway, flag ripple, selection pulse, march bob, casualty fade) is suppressed under `reduceMotion` — the STATIC ground texture stays (faithful detail, not motion; the T17 precedent). `renderRich="off"` disables the whole layer (motion reverts mid-battle; the 3D ground tint reverts on the next launch — the T16/T17 apply-time pattern, documented). The woods sway recomputes each instance matrix from a cached base (no drift); `fldLow()` trims sway amplitude + grain cell size; the **2D field-grain is cached to an offscreen canvas** (built once per field/scale, blitted with one `drawImage` — no per-frame fillrate on the weakest 2D-fallback GPU). No new draw call/shader → no `gl_PointSize` concern. CVD-safe (texture carries no colour-encoded info); no new DOM/text → `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern — 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity · render-math · perf · a11y-gating · edge-robust · lifecycle] × 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 37 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 substantive bug + 7 real LOWs, ALL FIXED:** **(the one substantive defect, MED/HIGH across 4 lenses, 3/3 votes)** the casualty-fade `g.position.y -= (1-rec.fade)*5` was CUMULATIVE — the base `fld3dSyncUnit` early-returns for a dead unit and never re-seats its Y, so the per-frame decrement compounded to ~125 yards of sink (frame-rate dependent), plunging the fading brigade through the terrain instead of the intended ~5yd settle → **rewritten ABSOLUTE** (`g.position.y = fldTerrainH(u.x,u.z)+4 - (1-f)*5`), bounded + frame-rate-independent (probe now asserts `maxSink ≤ 8`; measured 4.96). Pure visual glitch — no sim write, D74 intact (the finders + critic confirmed). **(LOW, real)** the fade had no visibility guard → a fog-hidden enemy that died popped into view as a fading block (a fog-of-war leak) → guarded on `rec.wasVis` (the base's last-living-frame visibility) + a white-box probe test. **(critic-found LOWs)** a SELECTED unit that died kept its ring at full opacity over the fading ghost → the ring now fades with the corpse; the fade-end `transparent=false` flip corrupted the textured T10 flag's alpha (latent) → `_rrSetGroupOpacity` never flips the flag/ring transparent flag; the 2D grain was re-filled (~1300 `fillRect`s) every frame → offscreen-canvas cache; `renderRich="off"` toggled mid-battle didn't revert the motion effects → the early-return was removed so the motion-off reset paths run; the probe only proved seed-stability (not sim-field invariance) → added the x/z/men/morale/facing snapshot; the empty-catch wrappers swallowed per-unit throws silently → a counted + once-warned `FLDRR_S.errN` the probe asserts is 0. **Probe strengthened 24→30 steps.**
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (module + 5 wrappers + chain markers · ground enriched [meanAbsDelta 0.0178, 92% of vertices changed] + positions untouched · woods sway/reset · flag ripple/reset · selection pulse · casualty fade visible+opacity-in-(0,1)+BOUNDED-sink+fog-ghost-guarded+hidden-when-done · sim seed + sim-field INVARIANT · `errN===0` · `renderRich="off"` un-enriched/unswayed/flat · reduceMotion keeps texture suppresses motion · 2D paints, 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity → combat byte-identical, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 coexists); `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17 coexists); `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (all 9 battles render, 0 texture warnings); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 0 fails/0 pe. ## D128 — PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") · H3-i2: **WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE** — procedural sky/light re-tint + rain/snow precipitation per a citation-grade per-battle weather hint — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The natural successor to H3-i1 (D127). A NEW presentation-only module gives each battle a sky and light that match its history. Designed + data-scoped at `.tmp/phase-h-design.md`. Continues leading Phase H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` — re-tints the 3D `scene.background` / `scene.fog` / sun (directional) / hemisphere AND washes the 2D canvas to a resolved `{sky, time}` palette (sky ∈ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow; time ∈ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk), plus optional procedural **rain/snow precipitation** (a second `THREE.Points` cloud reusing the T16 shader pattern) and a faint 2D precip hatch. A one-time accessible **weather note** is announced at battle start via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **Marquee visible win: Antietam's dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (the one genuinely non-clear sky in the roster); the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
- **ARCHITECTURE — combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dInit` (re-tint) / `fld3dRender` (precip + note) / `fld2dDraw` (wash + note) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16 seam; propagates T16's `._atmo` marker so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). Reads ONLY the scenario's structured `weather` hint (`_scenTop.weather` for multi-phase, else `scenData.weather`) + render state; its OWN LCG for the precip drift — **NEVER `fldRng`** (probe-asserted: the sim seed is untouched across a synchronous wx render loop); no sim write, no `_SAVE_VER`. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT:** a NO weather hint — or a `clear`/`midday` hint — resolves to `null` and applies ZERO change (every currently-shipped look is preserved until a battle opts in). Diff = `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T17 after T16) + the 9 `data/*.json` weather blocks + `tools/probe-weather.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat/save file touched.**
- **THE CITATION-GRADE DATA (research+verify Workflow, 18 agents: 9 Opus historians × 9 default-refute Opus verifiers):** each battle's documented modeled-window weather, ≥2 real sources, anti-fabrication. The verifiers earned their keep — they REFUSED to fabricate drama: Gettysburg `haze→clear` (Rev. Jacobs' instrument log: bright, 4/10 cumulus at the 2pm Pickett's-Charge window); Fredericksburg `fog→clear/afternoon` (the Rappahannock fog LIFTED ~10am, before the noon-to-dark assault — the note still teaches the morning fog that hid the crossing); Shiloh `clear/morning` (the famous torrential rain was OVERNIGHT, outside the modeled day); Vicksburg removed a misattributed Theodore Lyman source (an Army-of-the-Potomac aide, never at Vicksburg). **The honest finding: the "fog of war" at most of these battles was POWDER-SMOKE (already shipped via T16), not weather** — so the sky was usually clear; only Antietam's dawn fog is a real non-clear sky. Final hints: bullrun1 clear/afternoon · malvernHill clear/afternoon(Inferred) · **antietam fog/dawn** · fredericksburg clear/afternoon · chancellorsville clear/morning · gettysburg clear/afternoon · shiloh clear/morning · vicksburg clear/midday(a no-op) · chickamauga clear/afternoon.
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** the static sky/light TINT is faithful + motion-free → it applies under `reduceMotion`; only the PRECIPITATION (motion) is suppressed under `reduceMotion` (probe-verified: tint kept, no `wxPrecip` cloud). `G.settings.weather==="off"` disables the whole layer → the clear default. Fog far-plane held **≥1500** in EVERY palette (incl. the time blends) so the objective never vanishes (probe-asserted). One `THREE.Points` precip cloud (single draw call) + `fldLow()` budget (520/200) + a `gl_PointSize` clamp to the driver `ALIASED_POINT_SIZE_RANGE` max. Neutral atmospheric wash (no colour-encoded info → CVD-safe); no new DOM/text/interactive surface (the note reuses the AA-vetted `fldScenarioBanner`) → `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **DECIDED-&-LOGGED (D61) — Antietam's battle-level dawn-fog:** the fog/dawn hint is applied to ALL THREE Antietam phases (Cornfield → Bloody Lane → Burnside's Bridge), though historically the ground fog opened the Cornfield (Phase 1) and burned off by the later phases. Kept as the iconic, verified BATTLE SIGNATURE (the modeled engagement opens in the dawn mist, and the note teaches "it thinned as the sun rose"); per-phase weather would touch the T8 combat-path phase view (`_fldPhaseView`) and is logged as a clean future H3-i3 enhancement, NOT this milestone. The bug-hunt verifiers SPLIT on this (no majority-confirm) → a simplification, not a defect.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity/RNG · lifecycle/GPU-leak · WebGL1/r128 shader · a11y/perf/fog-readability · robustness/edge · effect-correctness+history+probe-rigor] × 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; the critic leg STALLED after the finder+verify phases completed — substituted by a rigorous INLINE completeness pass, the D124 precedent). **8 findings; 1 HIGH confirmed, fixed; the rest LOW/refuted, addressed:** **(HIGH, 3/3 confirmed)** the atmosphere note re-fired EVERY render frame — `_wxLaunchKey` included `__FIELD.seed`, which `fldRng` MUTATES every sim tick → the per-launch key changed each frame → the "noted" flag reset → banner/SR-status spam. **FIXED:** key the note on the STABLE `__FIELD.scenario` (fldExit resets it for a relaunch) + a new probe assertion that renders sim-ticking frames and asserts EXACTLY ONE weather banner. **(LOW, real)** `FLDWX.SKY["constructor"/"__proto__"]` resolves an inherited `Object.prototype` member (truthy) → bypassed the `!FLDWX.SKY[sky]` guard → a palette with no `.bg`. **FIXED:** `Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(...)` validation + a malformed-input probe assertion. **(LOW/refuted, locked anyway)** precip-dispose-on-`fldExit` + malformed-input safety were un-probed → added assertions; the `fld3dDispose`-wrap finding was refuted 3/3 (T17's `fldExit` wrapper runs `fldWxDispose` BEFORE the engine teardown; the scene-traverse disposes the mesh regardless; a stale ref self-heals on next build). A real **probe test-pollution bug** (the synth scenes mutated the SHARED `GAME_DATA` weather object, clobbering a later scene's pristine hint) was caught by the note-once assertion and fixed (inject onto a shallow copy).

UI-only attribute change in the picker render → combat byte-identical (`probe-presets` 26/26 NEUTRAL byte-identity GREEN; the full no-regression suite GREEN; `probe-realism-teaching` 12/12). Diff = `src/tactical/T6-presets.js` + `tools/probe-realism-teaching.mjs` + the generated HTML. (Reversible.)

## D121 — E2 increment 2: **THE INLINE GLOSSARY** — hover/tap/focus codex definitions woven into the teaching prose — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped:** the second E2 / S4-education item — an INLINE GLOSSARY. New `src/93-glossary.js` DOM-decorates the rendered teaching prose of the two read-only teaching desk tabs (After-Action, Your War vs History): a TreeWalker wraps codex terms in inline `<button class="gl-term">` triggers (a dotted brass underline) and a shared `#glTip` tooltip shows the definition on hover/focus/tap. It reads the SAME codex data as the i1 Codex tab (`cxGlossaryIndex`/`cxLookupShort`) — one source of truth. Hooked into `_wdRefresh` (guarded, scoped to afteraction/warvshistory), byte-identical when absent.
- **ACCESSIBILITY-FIRST:** the definition rides each trigger's `aria-label` ("<visible matched text> — <short> (glossary term)") so a screen-reader announces it on FOCUS regardless of the visual tooltip; the tooltip is `aria-hidden` role=tooltip decorative reinforcement (no double-announce). Triggers are real keyboard-operable `<button>`s; Esc dismisses; a scoped `:focus-visible` ring; reduce-motion disables the tooltip transition; the cue is a dotted UNDERLINE (shape), not color-alone. wcag-auditor AA (tooltip 13.51:1, term/border 8.10:1; no edits).
- **Surface-derivation (the keystone design):** matchers are built from DERIVED SURFACES, not the raw `en.term` — the core noun phrase (leading "The " + trailing "(...)" clarifier stripped), any parenthetical acronym (e.g. "(USCT)" → USCT), and authored aliases — so the spellings prose ACTUALLY uses match (e.g. "The Lost Cause (Myth)" → "Lost Cause"; "United States Colored Troops (USCT)" → "United States Colored Troops" + "USCT"). High-value bare-form **aliases** added to 3 codex entries (emancipation, blockade/Anaconda Plan, conscription/draft) — pure data the codex already supports.
- **Architecture — PURE READ-OUT (byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION):** `glDecorate` reads `GAME_DATA.codex` (via cx accessors) and DECORATES already-rendered DOM; it WRITES NOTHING to the sim (no campaign state, no save, no RNG). No tactical/combat/tick/resolve/bridge path references `gl*` (grep-confirmed + a probe static-scan over 20 combat files) → battles byte-identical by construction. The `_wdRefresh` hook clears `data-gl-done` before each render (the reused `#wdContent` element) so re-viewing a teaching tab re-decorates. Diff = `src/93-glossary.js` + `data/codex.json` (3 aliases) + `src/00-manifest.json` (`93-glossary.js`) + `src/30-president-shell.js` (the guarded hook) + `tools/probe-glossary.mjs` + the generated HTML.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (OFFLINE, no-internet per Aaron's mid-run pause; 5 diverse-lens Opus finders × default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 26 agents) → critic invariantsHold=FALSE initially (a genuine word-boundary bug), 16 confirmed findings, ALL FIXED + probe-locked:** **(the keystone)** the trailing `\b` made every term ending in `)` (USCT, the Lost Cause, Contraband, etc.) a DEAD matcher → fixed by the surface-derivation above (clean word-char-bounded surfaces); only-ONE-term-per-text-node dropped other terms → now wraps every distinct term left-to-right via a fragment; the aria-label led with the canonical (not visible) text → now leads with the matched text (WCAG 2.5.3); tap-on-term dismissed instead of revealed (touch users) → click now always reveals + click-outside dismisses; misleading comments corrected; and a PROBE-RIGOR cluster (the probe used a non-existent fallback term → always tested "Abraham Lincoln" and never a parenthetical term; the word-boundary test was vacuous; no event/skip-zone-completeness/multi-term coverage) → the probe rewritten to anchor on REAL derived surfaces (USCT/Lost Cause/Contraband/Anaconda Plan), test substring-rejection on a real surface, dispatch real focus/Esc/click events, cover all declared skip-zones, and the combat-path static-scan.

## D119 — E4-i2: **THE STRATEGIC WAR-END** — a reached `victoryReady` (a negotiated peace / a recognized independence) concludes the war via the graded report, for a victory that did NOT complete the battle chain — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the locked Phase-E item after E1):** the strategic arc's missing closure. Before D119 the war ended ONLY at battle-chain completion (`campaignAdvance` → `warWonScreen` at `idx>=chainLen`). Now a reached **`C.strategy.victoryReady`** — a **negotiated peace** (Northern/enemy will broken, `enemyWill≤30` in 1864+ or `≤18` any year) or a **recognized independence** (recognition ≥60, CS) — can CONCLUDE the war through the SAME D112 graded after-action report, surfaced as a **non-forced OFFER** on the between-battles interstitial ("The war can be concluded — accept the peace / claim independence", or fight on). This is the frozen campaign-loop closure the prompt named (E4-i2), built via the authorized `warWonScreen` override pattern (D116 authorized the frozen-loop override autonomously).
- **Architecture — an additive OFFER + the existing warWonScreen; byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION:** new pure helpers in `src/82-after-action.js` — `aarStrategicEndAvailable(C)` (returns `"will"` for either side / `"recognition"` **CS-ONLY** / null), `_aarEndFraming(C,reason)` (side-aware title/subtitle/verdict/offer copy), `aarStrategicEndOffer(C)`, `aarConcludeWar(reason)`. The `warWonScreen` OVERRIDE now frames the title/verdict via `_aarEndFraming`; at chain completion (`_aarEndReason` null) it is the **byte-identical D112 "The War is Won / Victory!"** screen with the base Main-Menu wiring + `G.campaign=null` preserved verbatim. The offer banner is one guarded IIFE in `_pdInterstitialHTML` (`src/20-president-render.js`) — returns `''` when no offer → **byte-identical interstitial** when `victoryReady` is null; wired (`#pdConcludeWar`) in `_pdShowTurnInterstitial` (`src/30-president-shell.js`). **No tactical file touched; no combat/tick/resolve/bridge path reads `aarStrategicEnd*`/`_aarEndReason`/`aarConcludeWar`** (grep-confirmed) → 9 battles byte-identical by construction. No new save state (`_aarEndReason` is a transient module var); NO `_SAVE_VER` bump; NO RNG.
- **SIDE-CORRECTNESS (anti-Lost-Cause):** `"recognition"` is gated **CS-only** — the Union never "wins" because the Confederacy gains recognition (D111 noted recognition is unreachable for US by normal play; the gate is the defensive belt). `"will"` is correct for either side (the enemy sues for terms), framed side-aware (US: "the rebellion lays down its arms"; CS: "Washington consents to let the South go"). A CS strategic victory is framed honestly as the survival of a slaveholding republic — never valorized — and the D112 graded report body carries the anti-Lost-Cause Reconstruction accounting (keyed on `victoryReady`, which `aarConcludeWar` does not clear, so the honest accounting renders correctly through the conclusion).

The LOCKED catalog (24 end-states + 7 axes + a labeled spectrum):
- **CONFEDERATE end-states (12):** (grounded→longshot) Recognized independence (the 1862 window won) · Negotiated peace 1864 (break Northern will to the election) · Emancipated Confederacy (Cleburne's path fully — independence but the founding creed gutted; anti-Lost-Cause, named honestly) · Stalemate / two Americas (an exhausted armistice) · Fabian survival (Johnston's pure-defensive attrition outlasts Northern patience) · Trans-Mississippi redoubt (Kirby-Smithdom survives west of the river) · King Cotton coerces Europe (the embargo finally pays) · The Northwest secedes (Copperhead success fractures the Union three ways). (fantastical) A British war (Trent escalates; the Royal Navy breaks the blockade) · Foreign legions land (Maximilian's army crosses the Rio Grande) · Stonewall lives (Jackson survives Chancellorsville) · The Golden Circle (a slave-power Caribbean/Latin-American empire).
- **UNION end-states (12):** (grounded→longshot) Reconstruction that HOLDS (the 14th/15th enforced past 1877 — no Jim Crow) · Early abolition war (1862) · Hard-war quick collapse (Sherman's doctrine early) · Reunion WITHOUT emancipation (the dark path — the war's purpose abandoned, named as the moral failure it is) · The 1862 knockout (Richmond falls early) · Forty acres enforced (emancipation + land redistribution carried through) · Compensated, bloodless end (Lincoln's road not taken — slavery ends by purchase) · The general strike triumphant (Du Bois's mass self-emancipation collapses the labor base). (fantastical/poignant) Lincoln lives Reconstruction (never assassinated; leads it himself) · The repeater/Gatling war (rapid-fire a year early) · A Russo-American century (the Tsar's fleet stays and fights) · The 13th early (abolition by amendment from the start).
- **REWARD AXES (7) — what "done right" unlocks the biggest divergences:** battlefield dominance · the economy/blockade game · the political/home-front game · the emancipation/manpower game · the command game (the GM depth-chart/rating system) · engineering & technology · intelligence & cavalry.
- **Wildness ceiling:** a LABELED SPECTRUM — grounded/plausible endings by default; fantastical endings unlocked by fantastical play and explicitly tagged "fantastical" (so the teaching line — what really happened — always stays clear). Honors the tiered wild-card design (D28) + the no-thumb-on-the-scale law (D54).
- **BUILD ORDER (Aaron):** **the FANTASTICAL tier FIRST** (the most fun/"video-game" payoffs), then backfill the grounded teaching forks. The end-state DETECTION + the ledger/report surfacing build on `divScan` (81-divergence.js) + the wild-card catalog (80-victory.js) + the `decResolve`/`_decApply` hinge-fork engine (32-decisions.js); each end-state carries a citation-grade counterfactual (the D111 inline-prose trust model; failures named both sides). Implement as vetted increments under E1; the actual war-END screens for these land with E4-i2.

## D113 — §12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND — a commissioned political general costs more capital to relieve before the 1864 vote (the bind Lincoln lived) — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the GM §12.3 keystone the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112):** a commissioned POLITICAL general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand — `commission.kind:"political"` + a `politicalValue`) delivers his constituency's votes to the war effort while he serves, so relieving him in the run-up to the 1864 election forfeits that support — an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set (the bind is spent). `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100) * windowByYear[year] * surchargeMax)`, bounded [0, surchargeMax=14]. A new teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost ("Lincoln lived this bind"). Teaches the §12.3 command-politics lesson concretely: Banks in command costs commandLeadership 49 vs Grant's 87 (D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864.
- **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log; the kickoff named it "pair with E4"):** chose the relief-bind over the frozen-loop negotiated-peace war-end (E4-i2) for an autonomous tick because it is a contained, well-authorized command-economy extension (the code already flagged it "the follow-on" at 35-command.js:985) with no frozen-loop touch and no design fork. Aaron then reordered the queue (E1 hinge-forks ahead of E4-i2); this D113 was already mid-vet so it lands first.
- **ARCHITECTURE — UNION-ONLY, byte-identical until you field a political general (D74 no-fudge):** new pure helpers `_cmdElectionBindCfg`/`_cmdPoliticalValue`/`_cmdElectionWindow`/`_cmdElectionSupportSurcharge`; `_cmdReliefCost` adds the surcharge. `_cmdReliefCost` is read ONLY by `cmdAppoint` (the relief economy) + `_cmdActiveCard` (display) — **NEVER by `commandLeadership` or any combat/bridge/tick path** (grep-confirmed) → the bridge + the 9 battles are byte-identical by construction. The surcharge is EXACTLY 0 for every starting-roster general (none is `commission.kind:"political"`), the entire CS side, and outside the window → `_cmdReliefCost` is byte-identical for the whole roster in every year; the only behavioral change is a UNION political general the player chose to commission AND field in the 1862-64 pre-election window. No new save state; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; NO RNG. Data: `ratings.json` `electionReliefBind` (surchargeMax 14 · windowByYear {1862:0.15,1863:0.45,1864:1.0} · prov Inferred + 2 real sources — McPherson, T. Harry Williams).

Critic confirmed NO-FUDGE holds (only `cmdAppoint`/`_cmdPoolHTML`/`_cmdActiveCard` read `_cmdReliefCost`; nothing combat) and the US framing is accurate + attributed.

## D110 — RATING SYSTEM **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER** (seat pool generals into division billets nested under a seated corps — the next rung of the GM depth-chart over the OOB tree) — [CODEX code + CLAUDE close-out] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The next rung of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.1's billet tree (Army → Corps → **DIVISION** → Brigade), built HIERARCHICALLY on the Q10 corps depth-chart (D108). Beyond seating the army's I–IV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **DIVISION** billets (3 per corps), spending `seatCost` (2) political capital (`C.clock.capital` — the existing GM currency, no new resource per §12). A division is staffable ONLY UNDER a SEATED corps (the real chain of command — a division belonged to a corps), so the depth chart becomes a TREE the President builds top-down.
- **PROVENANCE / CLOSE-OUT (the [AARON] hand-off):** the Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session, finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by **Codex** on this machine. Codex shipped a sound, builds-GATE-OK, byte-identical-to-source feature **but did NOT run the adversarial bug-hunt or write any doc trail** (a PROPER-VETTING gap vs CLAUDE.md #3 + a record-in-repo gap vs #5). This entry + the bug-hunt below are the **CLAUDE close-out** that brings D110 to the project's "done" bar. (No code was reverted — the commit is sound; this adds the missing vetting + documentation, plus the one bug-hunt fix.)
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only shape the army's LEADERSHIP facet — an INPUT the bridge already reads — via a small BOUNDED lift folded into `commandLeadership`, summed exactly like the corps lift: `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(Σ over seated divisions of (`effDivRating`−64)×`perSlotWeight`, ±`liftCap`) = clamp(Σ×0.03, ±2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his current grade is below `preferredGrade`. The lift is DELIBERATELY SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4, weight 0.03 vs 0.05) so the influence hierarchy holds — **army (~±17, §27) > corps (±4) > divisions (±2):** a lower tier is a smaller modifier, never dominant. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership → bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG.
- **THE GRADE-FIT (a division was a Maj. Gen.'s billet in BOTH armies):** `preferredGrade` is a bare Maj. Gen. for US and CS alike — distinct from the corps tier (a US corps a Maj. Gen.'s, a CS corps a Lt. Gen.'s). Many divisions were in fact led by Brigadier Generals early in the war, so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads `belowGrade` until promoted (the Q9 synergy, biting on both sides here). `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand`: perCorps 3 · seatCost 2 · preferredGrade {US,CS: "Maj. Gen."} · perSlotWeight 0.03 · liftCap 2 · belowGradePenalty 4 · **Inferred** · 2 real sources (Glatthaar, *General Lee's Army*; Weigley, *A Great Civil War*).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a division:** no division seated → the Σ is over zero slots → lift 0 → `commandLeadership` unchanged → the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf` (a vacant division contributes 0, NOT a penalty; `_cmdDivLift` has a fast-path returning 0 without walking the roster when `cmd.divisions` is empty/absent — so a pre-Q12 save with no record reads identically). **ONE BILLET PER MAN:** a general holds at most one of {army command, a corps, a division}; seating him in a division clears any corps/other division he held, and appointing/seating him HIGHER clears his division. **Vacating a corps CASCADES** — its orphaned divisions stop contributing lift, enforced at the READ layer (`cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift` filter divisions whose parent corps is no longer seated; `_cmdDivClean`:795 requires the parent corps seated) and cleaned on the next load-sanitize. `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:generalId}}` (nested) rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop array/non-object/out-of-range/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/dupes — the Q9/Q10/Q11 idiom). Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + `C.clock.capital`. Carries the Q9/Q10/Q11 hardening verbatim: the `isFinite` capital guard, the commission gate (`_cmdByIdRoster`+`cmdCommissioned`), and debit-the-rounded-gate-value.
- **THE TEACHING (anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** a corps was only as good as its divisions — A. P. Hill's hard-hitting "Light Division" and Hood's and Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions under Hancock's II Corps (Gibbon, Barlow)** — while a corps with weak divisions underdelivered. New UI: division sub-rows nested under each seated corps in the "The Corps Command — Depth Chart" section + a combined corps+division lift read-out; every new colour annotated ≥4.5:1 (WCAG-AA), every dynamic value `_cmdEsc`-escaped.

P. Hill's Light Division, Hood's, Pickett's) were **all-Confederate** while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier deliberately named both sides (the rout of Howard's XI Corps) — the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED (copy-only, byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow — accurate at Gettysburg/Wilderness/Spotsylvania) to both the player-facing `divFoot` string and the `divisionCommand` `_note`. The save-tamper lens independently executed an 18-vector battery against `_cmdDivClean` (Array/null/non-object/out-of-range/float-key/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/cross-corps-dupe) — all sanitize correctly; the no-fudge lens grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.divisions`; escaping confirmed safe (`htmlEsc` at render + `_cmdEsc` in the UI).

## D109 — RATING SYSTEM **Q11: THE COMMISSION MOVE** (bring documented POLITICAL GENERALS into the officer pool for political capital; the GM "Commission" move) — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart move of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.2/§12.3 ("Commission — bring a new officer into the pool"). Beyond the generals the war hands you, the President may now **COMMISSION the documented POLITICAL GENERALS** — US **Banks**, **Butler**, **Sigel**, **McClernand**; CS **Floyd**, **Pillow** — into his officer pool for **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` — the existing GM currency, no new resource per §12), after which they are appointable / promotable / seatable like any general. A new Command-desk **"Commission an officer — the political generals"** section lists each with his (LOW) combat OVR beside his (HIGH) political value, his constituency, an honest one-line record, and a Commission control (gated on capital + the `maxCommissions` slate). Teaches the GM layer's central command-politics lesson (§12.3, the keystone): political generals were **cheap to commission and weak in the field** — Lincoln and Davis took them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship — so once you appoint or seat one, his low OVR drags the army's leadership, the bind Lincoln lived. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose Commission (option C) over the symmetric AI-GM (B, [hard]) and the DIVISION sub-tier (B-alt, lower-risk-but-thinner) because it fills the GM layer's missing teaching keystone (the political-general bind the §12.3 anti-gamey constraints are built around), uses the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` byte-identical-until-used spine + the §8 person concept, and adds 6 new citation-grade historical figures. Scoped to a **pure pool-addition move** (no economy/election fork); the full §12.3 election-support relief-bind is logged as the explicit next increment (it needs the 1864-election state — here the relief COST is already taught via each officer's `relief` class through `_cmdReliefCost`).
- **ARCHITECTURE (byte-identical until the player commissions):** the commissionable officers live in a SEPARATE data array (`data/generals.json` → `sides[side].commissionPool`), so `_cmdSideGenerals` (the starting roster) and every byte-identity-critical path are UNTOUCHED. `cmdCommission` writes ONLY `cmd.commissioned` (an id list) + `C.clock.capital` + a reputation seed — NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). With nobody commissioned, `_cmdRosterPlusCommissioned` === the bare roster (`roster.concat([])`), so the appoint/promote/corps pools, `commandLeadership`, and the 9 battles are identical to HEAD `8eb913a`. A commissioned officer reaches the fight ONLY by being appointed/seated like any general — no new combat read. `_cmdById` was widened to also resolve the commission pool (so a commissioned-then-appointed officer resolves everywhere); `_cmdByIdRoster` keeps the roster-only lookup for the byte-identity-critical seeds + the commission "not-a-roster-id" guard. `cmd.commissioned` rides the save; `cmdInit` seeds `[]` once + SANITIZES on load (drop dupes / bogus ids / roster ids / over-cap; non-array → array — the Q9/Q8b/Q10 idiom). NO `_SAVE_VER` bump. NO RNG.
- **THE TEACHING (rank ≠ competence; anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** the 6 are authored with LOW combat OVR / HIGH political value — appointing a commissioned Banks fields commandLeadership **49** vs Grant's **87** (probe-verified). Honest records name the failures plainly on BOTH sides (Banks/Red River, Butler/Fort Fisher, Sigel/New Market, McClernand/Vicksburg insubordination; Floyd & Pillow/the Fort Donelson flight) AND credit the genuine contributions (Butler's 1861 "contraband" decision; Banks's Louisiana free-labor/emancipation work). The combat ratings are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading); the biographies carry ≥2 real published sources each (gate-4e-clean). ## D108 — RATING SYSTEM **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART** (seat pool generals into corps billets over the D106 OOB tree; the GM depth-chart MOVE) — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart MOVE of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.1/§12.2/§12.4 ("an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), the President now SEATS pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (I–IV Corps) over the D106 OOB tree, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` — the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource per §12). A new Command-desk **"The Corps Command — Depth Chart"** section lists the 4 billets, each showing its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization — Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps against the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard] — an enemy-command shadow wired to combat risks byte-identity/no-fudge) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + the side-aware grade-fit.
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` — an INPUT the bridge already reads — via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating − 64) × perSlotWeight, −liftCap, +liftCap )` (perSlotWeight 0.05, liftCap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, which already carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** `preferredGrade`. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership → bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe — NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (`(rating−64)×0.7`, swing ~±17); the corps lift (±4) is a secondary modifier (§27: small, never dominant).
- **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise, the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Major General's** command; a CS corps a **Lieutenant General's** — the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade by Act of Sept. 18, 1862 and promoted Longstreet/Jackson that October to command the ANV's new corps (formally organized GO No. 6, Nov. 6, 1862). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps (he leads stretched); promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. On the US roster every named general already meets the Maj. Gen. floor (a correct latent guard for any future junior/commissioned officer). `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand` block: `slots 4 · labels [I..IV Corps] · seatCost 3 · preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.", CS:"Lt. Gen."} · perSlotWeight 0.05 · liftCap 4 · belowGradePenalty 6 · prov Inferred · 2 real sources` (Sears 1988 on AoP corps creation; Glatthaar 2008 on ANV corps).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until the player seats a corps:** no corps seated → the SUM is over zero slots → lift 0 → `commandLeadership` unchanged → the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7`. A vacant billet contributes 0 (NOT a baseline penalty — that would break byte-identity). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` SANITIZES a stale/tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; array→{}). Constraints: one corps per general (reassign clears the old slot); the army commander cannot also hold a corps (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears the appointee's corps); seating gates on capital and debits the SAME rounded value the gate compared (the Q9/Q8b hardened idiom); vacate is free; re-seating the same slot+general is a no-op (no re-charge). New fns (`src/35-command.js` Q10 block): `_cmdCorpsCfg`/`_cmdCorpsSlots`/`_cmdCorpsLabel`/`_cmdCorpsPreferredGrade`/`_cmdCorpsClean`/`cmdCorpsSeated`/`_cmdCorpsBelowGrade`/`_cmdCorpsEffRating`/`_cmdCorpsLift`/`cmdCorpsCommanderFor`/`_cmdCorpsPoolFor`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdVacateCorps`/`_cmdCorpsSelect`/`_cmdCorpsSlotRow`/`_cmdCorpsDepthHTML`; edits to `commandLeadership` (+the lift term), `cmdInit` (seed+sanitize), `cmdAppoint` (clear billet), `cmdRenderTab`/`cmdWireTab`. NO RNG.
- **THE OOB-BOARD DISPLAY JOIN (T15, pure display):** seated commanders NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the D106 board (`fldCampaignOOB` attaches `co.commander` when `player.source==='derived'`; `_fldOOBSideExact` renders it). The predicted EDGE is UNCHANGED by seating (leadership is captured in the actual fight, never double-counted on the board). Authored battles show the historical brigades (no corps-slot naming); the enemy is NEVER named by the player's depth chart.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity · economy/determinism/bounding · citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers · XSS/escaping · UI/WCAG/edge] × default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; **11 agents; 5 raw → 3 confirmed (1 MED + 2 LOW); invariantsHold = TRUE** — the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.corps`, seat/vacate write only `cmd.corps`+capital, byte-identity airtight, no fabricated officers, the 2 sources real + on-claim). **ALL 3 confirmed FIXED:** **(MED, UI)** the seat event-log said "he leads **above** his grade" for a BELOW-grade general (contradicting every other surface) → "below". **(LOW, anti-fabrication)** the OOB-board attach was keyed by array index, so a real general could be named over a derived **"Garrison"** node (a sub-1200-man fort/detachment, NOT a corps billet) → the attach now guards to `/ Corps$/`-labeled nodes only (a probe assertion locks the Garrison guard). **(LOW, citation)** the teaching copy said the CS "created the Lt. Gen. grade in October 1862" → corrected to the precise Sept. 18, 1862 authorization + the October promotions + the Nov. 6 reorganization (in `data/ratings.json` + the `35-command.js` comment). The 3 critic-"missed" were non-blocking: the workflow agents could not run the browser probes (the main session ran the full suite — see below); the ±4 cap is secondary to the army-commander's ±17 (§27 holds); and probe step #5 already proved `cmdPromote` reaches Lt. ## D107 — RATING SYSTEM **Q8b: THE BETWEEN-BATTLE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE** ("scout the enemy" — tier-reveal the enemy OOB, scaled by the appointed general's cavalry) — [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §15; deferred at D100 until the D106 OOB-mapping substrate existed). On the President's-Desk Command tab, an **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the D106 Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` — the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote`; no new resource per §12) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. Teaches that good cavalry leadership buys good intelligence — Stuart's reconnaissance rides, and the catastrophic intelligence vacuum at Gettysburg when his cavalry was absent (named as a real Confederate command failure, not glorified). **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** both the GM depth-chart MOVES and Q8b scouting were unblocked by D106; I chose scouting over the depth-chart MOVES because its scaling input (the `cavalry` persona attribute, spread 50–70 across the 9 generals) and its `reveal` hook in `fldCampaignOOBHtml` BOTH already existed, `36-camp.js` explicitly deferred scouting to exactly this substrate, the D106 board already advertised a dead "Scout the enemy" CTA, and scouting is **pure display + an economy spend (never touches combat)** — the safest possible byte-identity. The corps-billet depth-chart MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks (bigger surface) — deferred next.
- **THREE RECON TIERS (§15):** **light** (unscouted — the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough brigade count + the CTA) → **better** (scouted, cavalry < `cavalryFullThreshold` 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, NO per-brigade detail) → **full** (scouted, cavalry ≥ 65: the complete enemy OOB, the exact view). With the 9 generals' cavalry: Grant (66) + Lee (70) → full; the rest → better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry (not a flat baseline). Intel is **fresh per engagement** — the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id, so it reverts to light when the battle changes.
- **ARCHITECTURE (the D106 wall preserved):** the WRITE (`cmdScout`) lives in `src/35-command.js` (it gates on capital like `cmdAppoint`, reads the appointee's `cavalry` via `_cmdGenPersona`, computes the tier via the pure `_cmdScoutTierForCavalry`, and writes ONLY `cmd.scout` + debits `C.clock.capital` — NEVER the scoreboard); **T15-oob.js stays a PURE READ-OUT** — `fldCampaignOOBHtml(C, {reveal, reconHtml})` is told the tier + the recon-control HTML by `cmdRenderTab`, and only ADDS the "better"-tier renderer (`_fldOOBSideScouted` + `_fldScoutPosture`). No combat/resolve/tick/conditioning path reads `cmd.scout` (grep-confirmed) → a campaign that never scouts is byte-identical to the pre-Q8b build, and the 9 tactical battles are untouched. Build-gate 4d already scans both `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`. `cmd.scout` rides the save (C.president serialized wholesale); `cmdInit` lazily sanitizes a malformed/tampered record (drop→null; valid→bounded) — no `_SAVE_VER` bump. Data: a `scout` config block in `data/ratings.json` (cost 3 · cavalryFullThreshold 65 · baselineCavalry 54 · 2 real sources). NO RNG (deterministic).

## D106 — RATING SYSTEM **THE OOB-MAPPING SUBSTRATE** + a read-only Order-of-Battle board (the §12.1 roster screen; the shared blocker for the GM depth-chart MOVES + Q8b scouting) — [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The shared plumbing the GM depth-chart MOVES (§12.2) and Q8b SCOUTING (§15) both depend on: a READ-ONLY layer mapping the strategic next-battle (`_brgNextBattle`) to a STRUCTURED order of battle — commander → corps → brigade — for BOTH sides, each billet carrying its OVR/grade/strength/provenance (the T14 rating spine). New module **`src/tactical/T15-oob.js`** (spliced after T14; `fldOOBForSide`/`fldCampaignOOB`/`fldCampaignOOBHtml` + helpers). Surfaced as a new **"Order of Battle — the Next Engagement"** section on the President's-Desk Command tab (one render line in `cmdRenderTab`). The recommended-but-FORK-RISKY item was scoped SMALL first per the run plan: a read-only query layer + roster board, **no combat wiring** (the procedural skirmish `_fldCampaignSkirmishParams` is UNCHANGED). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN §12.1/§13/§15. **No new fork surfaced** — `BATTLES[]` already carries real `cmdUS`/`cmdCS` per battle and the 9 scenarios carry real brigade OOBs, so the substrate is buildable read-only + citation-clean without contradicting a shipped teaching.
- **TWO SOURCES, ONE SHAPE:** a battle WITH a hand-built tactical scenario (`fldScenarioData`) exposes its REAL brigade OOB (real commanders + the authored provenance read straight from each unit note via `_fldOOBProvFromNote`, reusing the Q7 reader `_fldOOBUnits` which scopes a multi-phase battle to phase 0); a procedural battle DERIVES a deterministic corps/brigade tree split from the authored totals (`bd.us`/`bd.cs`/year), seeded by id+side (NO RNG). Derived billets are FORMATION-LABELED (I Corps · 1st Brigade · Garrison) with `commander:null` — **NEVER a fabricated officer** (CLAUDE.md #4 / D92). The army-commander headline names only the player's APPOINTED general (the GM payoff + his `_cmdGenRating` OVR) or the battle's historical `cmd<Side>` (BATTLES — Verified). NEVER invents.
- **THE WALL (D74/D94/D92):** a PURE READ-OUT + DISPLAY, called ONLY from `cmdRenderTab` — never a resolve/tick/conditioning path. Writes NOTHING; read at no point in combat resolution → the sandbox + all 9 battles are byte-identical **BY CONSTRUCTION** (the generated html diff vs committed HEAD `7df4372` is ALL-ADDITIONS — the T15 block + one desk-render line, **ZERO removed/modified lines**). build-gate 4d's `RATING_MODULES` now ALSO scans `tactical/T15-oob.js` (the no-fudge OUTPUT-WALL structural over it too).

The substrate returns the FULL data for both sides (so the GM/scouting can query it); only the BOARD gates the enemy. Triple-encoded + CVD-safe (OVR = number+letter+word; provenance = hatch+glyph+word; the edge = a labeled % bar); all data names routed through `_fldOOBEsc` (XSS-safe).
